# Thread: Greetings, everyone!

### Cicero106 — 2024-04-02T16:51:23+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/greetings-everyone.28742/post-333135>

I am a 21 year old med-student in Salzburg, Austria and in search of the truth about health and the correct way to live for a human being, which means following the true laws of nature. Fortunately, I was influenced by my father, a physician, who started to drift away from centralized medicine and introduced me and my mother (physician as well) to a different way of thinking. He started with diet and gradually moved up the hierarchy of importance concerning human health, first studying the work of others, for instance Alexander Wunsch and then discovering the work of Dr. Kruse.

I myself am following a carnivore diet, although I am convinced that diet is ancillary/secondary, because I am not living under optimal conditions (EMF, blue light) and well, maybe I got brainwashed a bit too much by the "meat-heads". The more I follow Dr. Kruse, the more I reorganise my priorities and the more I get a deeper and better understanding of what is fundamental. I am eager to learn and acquire as much knowledge as I can, in order to better explain to the people (my loved ones, patients, other physicians, as many people as I can) how they can reach their maximal state of health and well-being, simply by doing what nature designed us to do. Thus, in other words, I want to teach them to make me jobless.

### [Dr. Jack Kruse](https://www.facebook.com/drjackkruse/posts/the-impact-of-blue-light-and-late-night-eating-is-connected-to-the-fatty-liver-a/1175202442544108/)

The impact of blue light and late-night eating is connected to the fatty liver and metabolic syndrome because gut bacteria become more active and releasing more light while lowering melatonin levels?...

 www.facebook.com

**"Brain clocks that ensure the circadian control of food intake include a master light-entrainable clock in the suprachiasmatic nuclei of the hypothalamus and secondary clocks in hypothalamic and brainstem regions.**

### [The circadian regulation of food intake - PubMed](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/31073218/)

Feeding, which is essential for all animals, is regulated by homeostatic mechanisms. In addition, food consumption is temporally coordinated by the brain over the circadian (~24 h) cycle. A network of circadian clocks set daily windows during which food consumption can occur. These daily windows...

 pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov

### Brent Patrick — 2024-04-16T02:41:27+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/new-to-uncle-jacks-teachings.28783/post-333608>

**“The late-evening snack session resulted in less lipids oxidized than in the breakfast session,” said Kelly. “This confirms that the timing of meals during the daytime and night time cycle affects how ingested food is used versus stored, and that any food ingested prior to bedtime will delay the burning of fat during sleep.”

''the daily timing of nutrient availability coupled with the body’s increased metabolism during sleep (thanks to the body’s circadian rhythms) flipped a switch on fat burning''**

### [Fasting at night or in the morning? Listen to your biological clock, says new research](https://news.vanderbilt.edu/2020/02/27/fasting-at-night-or-in-the-morning-listen-to-your-biological-clock-says-new-research/)

According to a new study published by biological science researchers at Vanderbilt, the answer to eating (or fasting) windows lies in the circadian rhythms of the body’s biological clock.

 news.vanderbilt.edu

# Thread: Hello from the 36° N Latitude
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-from-the-36%C2%B0-n-latitude.28786/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 7
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### KellyMonroe — 2024-04-14T05:11:29+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-from-the-36%C2%B0-n-latitude.28786/post-333570>

Howdy! I’m from Hollister, California—we live in a farming community with about 37,000 people spread out across a large area. I’m 57 years young.

I’m here to trade in my insomniac card for a mitochondriac card. I haven’t slept all night in 15 years, it really sucks. Centralized medicine only offered me pills—I “politely” declined this so-called-lution.

I tripped across Uncle Jack’s body of work and knew he knows a lot of shit that’s super important to my sleep—and sooo much more. I found this info during a nightly learning time (aka during the middle of the night while awake—yeah yeah I know the blue light is a major player in my problem, but I didn’t know that then).

For last 3 weeks, I’ve dutifully witnessed the sunrise—even standing in the rain this morning I’m glad the farm workers weren’t working this morning…they’d have had quite the chuckle at this site.

Cutting iPhone/iPad/giant-ass tv time substantially has been an unexpected win—I feel calmer and very focused. Who knew?

I bought red lights for our bedroom—keeps the neighbors wondering and it’s so relaxing.

Something quite amazing is happening—I’m actually tired and sleepy at 7:30 pm! I fall asleep by 8:30 pm every single night. Definitely no complaints here.

Staying asleep is an issue—but I have faith that if I keep at it, there’s a solution. I’m awake for 1-2 hours nightly but going to sleep early means I feel better with 7.5 hours of totally sleep.

Oh, one more thing, I’m not crazy carb anymore—that’s crazy good in itself!

Another plus, my brain feels about 15 years younger and I’m not searching for words in every conversation. Here’s to more progress as I implement each step. ❤️

# Thread: Zoran presentation
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/zoran-presentation.28871/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 4

### Zoran_Seremet — 2024-05-09T00:33:25+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/zoran-presentation.28871/post-334495>

Hi there! My name is Zoran, and I'm living in Catalonia,Spain. I began delving into some unconventional health practices after being diagnosed with type 2 diabetes in October 2022. Concerned about my health, I decided to make changes to my lifestyle, one step at a time.

I started by adjusting my diet, cutting out processed foods, and embracing a low-carb approach. But I didn't stop there! I also began soaking up as much sunshine as possible, paying attention to my circadian rhythms, taking cold baths, interment fasting, and grounding.

As time went on and I continued learning and applying new knowledge, I began to notice a significant improvement in my energy levels and motivation. And here's the best part - my type 2 diabetes vanished within the first 6 months! I never had to take any medication; all it took was a change in my diet.

Now, I feel better than ever, and I'm excited to keep exploring new ways to improve my health!

> and embracing a low-carb approach

Spend some time thinking about carbohydrates.
Not all carbohydrates are the same.
Some raise glucose faster, other do that slower.
Make sure that you eat them least processed possibly.
Eating a whole grain of wheat is one story.
Eating just white flower from the same grain of wheat is something else.

Drink only plain water.
All drinks are usually sweetened with fructose.
Higher amounts of fructose are especially bad news, especially for some people.
It raises uric acid in some of them.
Make sure to find out your blood uric acid content.
The best should be about 3 to 4.
Higher will cause many problems, weak joints, osteoporosis, many other
Too low uric acid ---> Parkinsons

////////
Eventually you want
first:
Body temperature 36.6C to 37C
then
fasting insulin of zero to 5
fasting glucose 90
uric acid 3-4

/////

# Thread: Ahoy from New England
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/ahoy-from-new-england.28874/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 2
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### jinqui — 2024-05-09T19:35:13+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/ahoy-from-new-england.28874/post-334527>

Ahoy from New England, I'm fired up to be here. I’ve come to uncle Jack’s teachings by necessity like many others to try and heal from chronic ailments. I was a D1 athlete and attending an Ivy-league university when my health collapsed, and I’ve been on a medical leave ever since. After running through the medical industrial gauntlet, I’ve been diagnosed with a host of diseases (primarily Lyme & Coinfections, CIRS/Mold toxicity, auto-immunity, and chronic encephalitis). It’s been quite debilitating and over the last 5 years I’ve been far and wide looking for answers. I’ve done just about every one of the textbook appropriate testing/imaging and treatments but have found no progress.

I’m really not one for diagnoses because while they can be useful, I’ve found that trying too hard to label my disease has obfuscated my understanding of the bigger picture at hand; Looking too specifically for the causation and not for the correlation. I’m beginning to realize I might be missing some critical component or components, hence why I’m here.

The multi-disciplinary approach of Dr Kruse immediately appealed to me (drawing on biology, physics, history, philosophy & chemistry to name a few). After seeing this perspective it’s hard to understand anything again in disease as occurring in isolation or being non-relative. Lastly, while I’ve been doing my light, water, & magnetism homework I’m still pretty green and haven’t yet started to translate any of these ideas into practice. I’m excited to learn with you all, and I hope I can be of some help.

### Chozami — 2024-05-15T17:47:21+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/ahoy-from-new-england.28874/post-334740>

I'm in MA, near the RI border, and in a similar position. I've not done as much testing/imaging as you and I'm interested in learning more about CIRS/Mold toxicity because I've never really considered it for myself. I just so happened to find biotoxin.com yesterday and I joined this forum today. Currently I'm working on Gene test interpretation to make determinations about my health.
We should dive in deeper sometime.

Hi everyone,

I am a personal trainer & dietitian from Athens/Greece. I've been in this amazing journey of improving body composition and health for over 30 years now and I absolutely love this!
Being adjective and suspicious as a person about almost every "mainstream" advice and directives, I always try to read between the lines and have an open mind about learning.
Having learned from some of the best in the field and having the drive to learn more, I "accidentally" fell upon Dr. Jack Kruses' name from a podcast of someone I follow and respect.
After listening to the two-part podcast with Rick Rubin & Andrew Huberman, my mind had expoled and my jaw dropped with what I heard. What a great perspective, a whole new window of knowledge has opened and much more reading and studying for me!
In many ways, Dr. Kruses' approach "explains" and "verifies" much of what I've learned in all these years; things that I thought were somehow radical and controversial and only believed because I highly trusted the man behind (just for the shake of conversation and respect the man was Charles Poliquin).
So, here I am and looking forward to expand my knowledge with all you amazing people!

# Thread: Out in the open
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/out-in-the-open.29130/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 3
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### Uswebers1 — 2024-07-11T04:46:03+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/out-in-the-open.29130/post-336937>

Hi,

This is my story and I’m sticking to it. I am 6’2” at the moment BMI 27.0
I am 2/3 to 71 times around the sun.
I grew up on L.I., NY, Jones Beach was part of my childhood. At 18 I left and spent the next 4 years in the USN between California and Vietnam on an Aircraft Carrier, and beaches inbetween. After my time spent I worked outside installations, in Silicon Valley, California, for about 6 years. Moved to inside work for about asa Machinist, but with the internet as and fast, cheep overseas turnout, machine shops were laying off and closing the doors. Getting tired of getting laid off i got a job delivering mail for Uncle Sam. My dream job returned in aways wanting a job i could work out side. Starting at 52 years of age I’ve just about hit 20 years.
i am mostly Norwegian and English, my mtDNA is H. I have had dirty blonde hair, now gray/blonde. My eyes are green. I have had a BMI of around 30.0 for most of this time. I went strict dietary Vegan for 8 years, eating vegan cookies and cakes along with some good veggies, until 2013. I think this is what set me up for future failure. Then after a couple of Hawaiian Luaus i went SAD diet. In 2018 i got keto fever with the keto junk and some good food. Then i cane across Dr Paul Saladino just as he started his Carnivore, and followed him into fruit and honey. I didn’t take the Jab. I like science, I’m not all that smart, so when I heard it was this new kind of Jab, i was very interested. Well after i found out what it was i said no you’re not messing with my DNA. Plus i was listen to Alex Jones.
Well anyway lI walk 14 miles (30,000steps) house to house 5 days a week in a Mediterranean type climate, with shorts all year long. Plus i stopped using Sunscreen a out a year ago. My glasses are UV block reading glasses.
So i started years ago can’t remember, maybe around 50 having BPH problems. Getting close to a pill to pee but managing through some magnesium at night and trying to figure out what foods to eliminate. So 20 years later my PSA is 9.?, i did the biopsy a couple of years ago and got really nausea during the experience. It was clear. So they have been bugging for another. I read up and finally talked them i to an MRI so if it was positive they would know were to poke. Well after all this medical malpractice and not wanted to be injected with radioactive die. I just leave them alone and ignore them. In the mean time I was studying up on cancer and anti parasitic drugs and teied bouts of 2 of them and it seems my urine volume got larger and my flow has really never been better in the revent past. Not having any inability to pee at night. Si naybe their is sime slow growing cancer involved as these Anti-parasitics help in cancer cell Apoptosis supposedly. Then I found thru my Food youTube addiction Dr. Jack Kruse, and i knew immediately that this guy was a genius, for putting it all together down to the light-electron-water-magnetism eureka moment. It all makes so much logical sense, even with my weakness in these combined sciences. So i think even though Iive and probably will remain here in this environmentally toxic jungle, I believe my health will improve. Already I don’t put my phone in my heart pocket anymore. i was already using sime amber lights at night, bu Dr Jack have been evolving, or is it deevolving my life style.
You k ow how when someone finds gold and they know they shouldn’t tell anyone, but because of their great excitement they can’t help but tell everyone? Now most everyone thinks I'm crazy. But I do find some intelligent folks
Thank you Dr Jack
Thank you Dr Jack
Thank you Dr Jack

Beautiful split-level share house in Mt Nebo, 25mins from Samford or The Gap. ### Johan Lindøm — 2024-08-22T10:00:59+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/meet-up-europe.29249/post-338779>

Madeira a geopathic stess zone? I do not thing so:

["Madeira Island is the emergent top of a massive shield volcano that rises about 6 km from the floor of the Atlantic Ocean and forms the largest island of the 90-km-long Madeira Archipelago. Construction of the volcano along E-W rift zones from the Miocene to about 700,000 years ago was followed by a period of extensive erosion and possible edifice collapse. Two steep-walled amphitheaters open to south in the central part of the island. Late-stage eruptions are scattered throughout the island and lasted until the Holocene, producing scoria cones and intra-canyon lava flows covering rocks of the older eroded edifice. The youngest activity lies in the west-central part of the island, and consists of cinder cones in the upper Sao Vicente valley, a series of intra-canyon flows, and a tephra layer on top of the Paul da Serra plateau dated at about 6,500 years ago."](https://volcano.si.edu/volcano.cfm?vn=382120)

Cape Verde a geopathic stess zone? I do not thing so: [The Cape Verde Islands were created by magma rising through the ocean, which is why they never were part of the African continent.](https://www.capeverde.com/country-info/volcanism) My biggest concern about traveling to Cape Verde is the American military. They have invested half a trillion dollars in military infrastructure, and a portion of these funds is certainly used for communication. However, I have not been able to understand how this affects the island of Santa Maria, where we will be spending New Year's.

Another vacation destination I am considering is Gambia in Africa. Flights are arranged there from Norway.

### Michalis — 2024-09-08T15:53:39+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/meet-up-europe.29249/post-339401>

You can use Xapo to buy bitcoins or alternatively use HodlHodl which is anonymous. You will pay more though. I think Xapo is a good solution as banks in the UK are blocking purchases. Ideally open a Xapo account and also open a Wise account as well.
Use the Wise account to transfer money from your legacy bank account to the Xapo account. Use it as a proxy in case your bank catches a whiff of what you are trying to to so be safe and continue buying.

As for meetups Fuertaventura looks great on paper. Actually I might be going soon if the plan I got for the winter falls through. La Gomera seems also good but a bit off the beaten track.

I do not have a map for antennas. I think it is much more effective to just not go to a very high population area (not big cities) and then testing anyways. Low pop generally only will provide low RF/MW but you still should really test for dirty electricity, electric and magnetic fields IMO (and testing also anyways RF/MW even if you go to a low pop place, since sometimes antennas can be hidden).

Yes I am Spanish, I live in this 250k city at the 43 latitude: [https://es.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oviedo](https://es.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oviedo)

I guess where I live is far from optimal in lower light months (november-february), so I would not recommend for living year around. I live here especially because of job, but I try to do very well other things, like CT, maximizing time outside, etc. Also that´s why I´m planning to do some winter vacations South and in the mid - long term moving South. But if anyone wants come visit and talk here I´m super happy.

Depends on your situation, but in the Mediterranean part of Spain the weather is much better, more Sun, etc. Places like Malaga, Alicante, Valencia, etc. I think are better than mine. [@metabolicdaria](https://forum.jackkruse.com/members/29467/) lives there so she may be able to tell you better. Even though they have more Sun, they have the sea, etc, those places are not super low lat, so maybe Canaries could be even a better idea. I think it depends a lot on your n=1. Also how much money you have is quite important. I have not been to the Canaries yet but I heard acommodation is getting quite expensive.

# Thread: Hello Everyone
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-everyone.29271/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 1
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### alleerielle — 2024-08-08T04:35:17+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-everyone.29271/post-338178>

I am so glad to be here. I have been reading as much as I can and listening to every Jack Kruse podcast I can find. There's so much to learn but it is so exciting and interesting. It definitely feels necessary.

In 2011, I was told I most likely have a rare blood disorder, Essential Thrombocythemia, which is a high platelet count. I never got it confirmed with a bone marrow biopsy because I didn't see the point of going through that hell for something that has no cure. I had an IV iron transfusion 2017 to see if that would get my platelet count down, however, it did not. Fast forward to today and my recent blood test showed all my blood counts are high, especially red blood cells. So I'm thinking I may have Polycythemia Vera instead. I am currently trying to find a hematologist that specializes in Myeloproliferative Neoplasms to find out.
[https://www.lls.org/myeloproliferative-neoplasms](https://www.lls.org/myeloproliferative-neoplasms)
Either way, I am committing myself to getting as healthy as I possibly can. I get morning sun everyday and get out in the afternoon to raise my Vitamin D levels. I'm also eating more seafood, which is just sushi right now. I know I need to try to expand my menu in that area. I wear my blue blocking glasses at night and am working on getting prescription ones for working on the computer. I just started drinking 125ppm deuterium water to see if that helps lower my blood counts. I just ordered Gabor Somalyai's book "Deuterium Depletion: A New Way in Curing Cancer and Preserving Health" which comes tomorrow. I have always hated sunscreen and sunglasses so my instincts were on point there. I have been a lifetime night owl and always wondered why I felt so awake at night. Now I know it was because I wasn't watching the sun rise. I feel silly that I never knew it was that simple and I am grateful that I know now. I still feel the urge to stay up, however, a lifetime of a lack of sleep and too much blue light has most definitely caught up to me. Melatonin is a priority now. Looking forward to connecting with like minded people here and of course I would love to hear any wisdom about my condition that anyone may offer. Thank you!

Greetings crew! I'm a new member, and making my first visit to El Salvador soon: Aug 20th to 29th!
I look forward to meeting other health-oriented folks and learning more about Bitcoin while I'm there.

I am staying at MT's place for most of this visit.

My hometowns in the U.S. are Dallas and Los Angeles and I'm looking to relocate for 3-6 months in El Salvador, Colombia, or Mexico in a peaceful, natural setting to do a **mold detox** wherever I land (I got very sick from being in moldy buildings).

Questions I have:

-   Are **saunas** easy to find in El Salvador, or should I just bring my portable infrared sauna? And is **cold plunge** a thing in El Salvador?
-   How is indoor **mold** in El Salvador? I've noticed it varies greatly across Latin America depending on environment and local practices.
-   For high quality olive oil, MCT oil, etc. do you fly back to the U.S. regularly to reload and put into checked luggage? Or **can you have items shipped to San Salvador efficiently**?

Additional info on me:
Being a perfectionist I don't call myself fluent in Spanish, but I can certainly get around and have lived in various Spanish speaking countries.

I'm an INFJ and when I leave my cave I love exploring various ideas and concepts in conversation with others...science, society, spirituality, etc. I get bored with small talk, gossip, and such conversation topics of most people. I prefer deeper, introspective and/or provocative topics that can lead to learning and growth vs. monotonous repetition of the same.

>
> _Isn't that a bit expensive for El Salvador? What would be a good price for a month?
>
> Are there other "mitofriendly" homes you know?
>
> Is it easy to get organic food there in Atami or in El Salvador in general?
>
> Is it possible to get water in glass bottles there or should I bring my activated carbon filter for the tap water?
>
> Who else is in Atami?_
>
> Best, Benne

Hello Benne,
Atami is a lovely place! I was there for 9 months but have currently moved to Shalpa where a friend, Jack McKenna, and I have have a house right across the road from the beach. We have a couple of rooms for rent if you still need a place. We are pretty hardcore “Mito” here with red lights and Ethernet cables only etc
Drinking water generally comes in BPA-free, plastic 5 gallon bottles.
If you would like more info feel free to private message me on here.
Hope your stay here is amazing!

# Thread: Hello from Northwest Indiana, the armpit of Chicago
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-from-northwest-indiana-the-armpit-of-chicago.29296/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 3
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### AustinBrewster — 2024-08-13T20:46:00+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-from-northwest-indiana-the-armpit-of-chicago.29296/post-338380>

Hello everyone, I am so happy jack punched me in the mouth a year or so ago, although I was looking for this punch of truth for a long time. When I started reading his blogs, I knew why his information had been hidden from me. I’ve always intuitively known there was a deeper level to everything in the universe and nature was the answer to it all. I have been obsessed with becoming a better athlete and seeking truth since I was 14. I became a registered nurse in 2018 and was professionally disappointed from the start, but got my degree because I knew I’d at least have financial stability and some free time. I have done a lot of my own research into biochemistry and the benefits of circadian biology and food from that lens. When my son had a seizure at 5 months old in February of 2023 and his Vit D came back at 18 and was positive for an MTHFR SNP, my world changed. My wife was breastfeeding at the time so we went strict carnivore for the rest of the winter together, supplemented him with Vit D and K2, as well as Methylfolate/methylcobalamin, gave him full spectrum CBD, and took him off his Keppra. He hasn’t had a seizure since that hospital visit, he turns 2 years next month. During that hospital stay the fire was lit inside me and I am getting emotional even writing this because of the anger, frustration, and sadness I felt for the next parent that would have no clue there is a deeper level to your child’s health problem that the pediatrics departments wont tell you about. No longer was I going to allow my lack of knowledge affect my family and my mind the way it was, and no longer could I hold up the lies I knew the doctors I worked next to go on. I became outspoken amongst my peers and in the hospital system this falls on deaf ears, but I am doing this for myself and for the ones that aren’t deaf. Since I “fixed” my sons seizures through these methods, I thought I was onto something amazing, and delved into the carnivore and keto rabbit hole. Huberman also helped me quite a bit. I justified it as the best possible diet for our health because I was buying grass fed local beef that I knew wasn’t raised with the standard care of beef. I thought it was the least toxic option we have since clean fruits and vegetables were harder to come by in my area. I stumbled upon jack through Sara Pugh’s YouTube channel among others a couple months after my son had his seizure. I heard, “he wont dumb it down for you” So I kinda played it off like it was too high level for me and I couldn’t understand it. (Low agency as f\*\*\*) I kept his name in the background, thinking “Ill get to his work one day”. Through my journey I decided to become a Nurse Coach, and honestly the program made me believe in myself because I saw a way to get paid for my knowledge not my time. Spring of 2024 I found decided to finally delve into his work by listening to the 10 hours of podcasting on Tetragrammaton. I can’t stop listening or reading his work. He is basically like google for the curious people, he really stimulates thinking. Since then, I have been doing everything I can to keep my family strong and healthy, protected from my shit environment. Luckily, I live in a rural area, but it is surrounded by glyphosate rich fields.

Hey AB-- I am originally from north central IN & a Purdue grad. I've been living by the ocean the past decade in NE Florida. Seeing the sunrise and sunshine daily is Huge, those grey sky months get tough up there. UV levels are tough, I believe that's why a lot of folks get addicted with going to the tanning salons up there, not just to look good but their bodies crave the UV.

With everything you guys got going on ^^ I would recommend relocating down here (or even further south). All of my family is still in Indiana, which can be tough, but if you moved beachside they will all have a reason to come visit you. It can give them something to look forward to. The attached photo is from my front porch overlooking the intracoastal & out to the Atlantic.

One of the best things you can do for your family is provide a positive environment for them. Chicago & "The Region" are definitely not that. Writing this note to be a resource of information for you, hope for the best for you and your family. You can message me directly if curiousity strikes. Cheers man......MM

### Mat.I — 2024-08-19T02:51:21+0300

I’m wanting to come to El Salvador next week, however I know it’s still rainy season. Is the health benefits still good during the rain or no? I’m assuming yes. Didn’t know how much the sun would be covered. Also I’m trying to get a consultation from Dr Kruse while I’m there

### Kirsten F — 2024-09-02T19:12:23+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/el-salvador-visit.29394/post-339167>

Hello, I am in ES and the sun is great. The most common pattern is sunny and beautiful in the mornings. If it does rain (we just had a few dry days), it is most likely that the rain clouds will gather in the mid to late afternoon.

### Ra Beam — 2024-09-02T19:23:53+0300

### Kirsten F — 2024-09-02T19:38:40+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/el-salvador-visit.29394/post-339170>

They still have seasonal rain storms (we had one for 7-8 days in June) where it rained nearly non-stop. I have heard that they are common in October as well. My vote is to not worry about it, come and enjoy. Other than that time in June, it has been beautiful despite being "rainy season".

Where are the beaches that aren't black sand in ES?
The black sand isn't too hot to be on. I recommend laying in the surf while you get sun.
Palmarcito is nice. Stay to the end of the beach where the Atami Resort is to avoid RF from the cell tower.
I like Shalpa. Less rocks than Palmarcito or Tunco.

# Thread: new member, in Brooklyn -- HELLO! :-)
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/new-member-in-brooklyn-hello.29396/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 2
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### meruprecht — 2024-09-02T20:30:29+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/new-member-in-brooklyn-hello.29396/post-339174>

Hello all, hello Dr. Jack Kruse,

Much thanks to Dr. Kruse for all your work and for creating this space. I am looking forward, as part of my journey to healthfulness and happiness, to being part of the community here and learning from folks. I am right now finishing Dr. Kruse's EXCELLENT book and have started my Lepsin Rx reset. Day Two. (I didn't need tests, I did what the doctor said, looked in the mirror and whoops, yep, obese person. ) My son is a big fan of Jack's, and he's the one who let me know about your/his work.

**My situation, health-wise:** I have struggled with obesity for the last 30 years, I just turned 63. I want to change my lifestyle, lose the weight, and be truly healthy for the duration. I was struck by the fact that Dr. Kruse's personal health journey started with weight gain AND a meniscus tear in the knee -- my story is much the same, and I imagine many peoples'. About ten years ago I tore the meniscus in my left knee, the first physical long-lasting debilitation I have had, other than the obesity. I need to lose around 133 pounds, and I now know, Jack, that you lost that amount too. So these parallels, as well as what I'm learning from the book, got me really interested, and now, started. I am, additionally, a dedicated intermittent faster, since 2022, and have always rejected (tried to reject?) the Western diet, which Jack calls SAD. (It is, sad! lol. I also teach Food Studies in my composition classes, which my students love, and which helps me stay on top of things somewhat.)

Also, I was diagnosed in 2021 with uterine cancer, whether it was pre-cancer or cancer I was never clear but the doc said the treatment is the same: full hysterectomy, plus some lymph nodes. After that I was declared by NYU Langone "cancer free," which I hope is fully true -- they said there was no spread, etc. What they did not tell me, and I only now know because a colo-rectal surgeon told me, is that after abdominal surgery people often develop gastro issues? Who knew. The colo-rectal surgeon told me that the uterus is a buffer for the colon, and that when you lose it your colon starts reaching out for other organs as buffers, and you develop "fistulae" (and there is another word he used), which I have. That diagnosis came after a diagnosis of diverticulitis, all of this following the hysterectomy. At the time, a year ago, I was told I needed colo-rectal surgery even though I have no pain and am asymptomatic generally. (The only reason this was diagnosed was because I got a CAT scan ordered by my gynecological oncologist, to make sure everything was good in there, but what it showed were these fistulae, so she sent me to the ER, a truly hell'ish night where they kept going back and forth, do I need emergency surgery or not? It was literal hell -- and, I had JUST had massively invasive surgery less than two years before that.) I felt at the time like jumping to surgery was too far of a leap -- and my doctor kept delaying the surgery, waiting for me to lose weight. Finally I said, if it can keep being delayed (twice), do I REALLY need this surgery? To which he said, Okay, no, let's put it off indefnitely unless I become symptomatic. I haven't.

All of what I am reading, Dr. Kruse, in your book is making me think about all this again. Do I have leaky gut actually? Do I have leptin resistance? Certainly I do, I must. And if I was to change my lifestyle, food intake, and all, as prescribed in the book and the Leptin Reset/PostReset, might my body repair itself through these natural means? Through autophagy? As you say, surgery without surgery. I have never been a believer in Western med., fully, I have never believed in popping pills to solve problems (unless truly medically necessary). My x-husband has terrible type 2 diabetes and takes all these meds which I fear are only making his sickness worse; having read the diabetes chapter last night, Dr. Kruse, I am sending him the book TODAY. (I already sent him _The Diabetes Code_ in response to which he changed nothing. Maybe this book will be the magic.) Anyhow -- that is just a bit about my health situation, why I'm here and reading the book and starting to make the prescribed/suggested changes.

**About me, as in my life:** In terms of my work, I am a professor and scholar, I teach at CUNY in Brooklyn, and I write and publish scholarly books, articles, chapters, alot of them , and the occasional Op Ed. (I'm an English prof., this is my page on MLA Commons: [https://mla.hcommons.org/members/meruprecht/](https://mla.hcommons.org/members/meruprecht/) ) I'm also a single mother, although my children are all grown up now, both in their 40's. My son owns two Brooklyn restaurants and he is very into Dr. Kruse and related; my daughter is a geoarchaeologist who does amazing work around cultural heritage rights for Native American communities.

As a final note, I've been thinking about how, when I was young I was never heavy, I was thin, fit, rode my bike for hours daily, climbed trees all the time, played softball---it was after a series of traumas leading up to losing my father in 1990 that, afterwards, I pretty much fell apart and started putting on this weight. But I've been thinking, along with all of what I have learned from Dr. Kruse, and hope to learn by being here, that we can re-find our original healthy selves, whether by that we mean "evolutionarily" or we mean literally our own life.

I am glad to be here, to have found Dr. Kruse's work, grateful also to my son for sending me this way -- and looking forward to learning everything Jack and everyone here will teach me, and also being a support to others however I can be.

Peace, love, solidarity--
~Maureen

So I sat in the sun eating breakfast.

# Thread: My Mid-Life Health Journey

### La-Shawn Hill — 2024-09-20T00:36:49+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/my-mid-life-health-journey.29465/post-339742>

Hello. My health issues began six years ago when I entered perimenopause. It was hard adjusting to HBP meds, for starters, but the real atomic bomb has been the toll perimenopause has taken on my mental health. I belong to a group of women referred to as "The Lost Generation." Even though I've always known I had an "attention problem," I wasn't formally diagnosed with ADHD until age 45 when "hor(ror)mones" took away my executive functioning and caused me to develop adrenal fatigue. We were all placed on lockdown during the pandemic. Well, once the lockdown was lifted, I found out just how "not okay" I still was due to my newfound anxiety and high-functioning depression. Perimenopause is harsh, but due to the severity of my mental health issues I wondered if perhaps I was suffering from Long COVID--or maybe even vaccine-injured. ADHD meds weren't helping me. I got tired of centralized medicine doctors and turned to functional medicine doctors. I eventually lost faith in doctors, period, and begin doing some hardcore health research of my own. Eventually I discovered the work of Dr. Kruse, and it made sense. I'd tried "talk therapy" for a time--it never helped. Actually, I'll say the one thing that did help me during my time in counseling was the advice to 'get out and walk' for my depression. Before that, I would literally work from sun-up to sundown inside my home office. Today, since becoming a follower of Dr. Kruse, I work outside on my porch. Can the sun really cure my body of what ails me? I don't know, but I'm here. And, I guess I'm not completely averse to centralized medicine since I just had an appointment with a new gynecologist. She says perhaps the HRT I tried in the past wasn't getting absorbed into the skin. There's a chance that HRT may help me yet. If not, it hurts nothing to improve my circadian biology by working on my light environment. If the sun and/or HRT don't fix me, then I have some other ideas as to what's going on with me. I'm open to any and all suggestions. Thanks in advance.

### SWDC — 2024-09-22T22:12:16+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello.29479/post-339847>

Greetings from the ruins of Lahaina.

I’m new to the party, only recently aware of your work through Nicole Shanahan’s “Council of the Cancelled.”

I’m struck by the similarity of your journey to that of George Crile, MD, early 20th century pioneer in surgical anesthesia and blood transfusion and one of the founders of the Cleveland Clinic.

In his quest to understand living processes he concluded that answers could not be found in biology so he turned to the study of physics.

He chronicled his research in his 1936 “The Phenomena of Life” and came to some big-picture similar conclusions, but without your advantage of a century of advancement in physics.

He’s too important of a figure to erase from medical history, so they just eliminate all references to his two works, “The Bipolar Theory of Living Processes” (1926), and the one mentioned above (available online as a .pdf).

Anyway, I look forward to learning and putting into practice what I am able to absorb here.

# Thread: Seems like everyone here is also inclined to seek the truth :)

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### jamesccg — 2024-10-12T23:15:55+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/seems-like-everyone-here-is-also-inclined-to-seek-the-truth.29601/post-340904>

Hi, I'm James. For years I've had instincts that cause distrust for modern mainstream healthcare - what I now know to be 'centralized medicine' - and I'm in admiration of Dr Kruse's efforts, along with the digital colony of 'Mitochondriacs' that seem to be growing here.

I found an unexpectedly inexpensive source of true 380nm UVB light, via the PeeDar 2.0 pet urine detection flashlight (it's part of their entire marketing campaign, as being better than 395nm - 400nm for detection, and so it appears to be a legit 380nm UVB source for only ~$20 on amazon) for stimulus to the Anabolic MTOR pathway. So I'll be able to at least provide a small trigger for cell repair, when not in ideal outdoor lighting conditions. However coming across 1280nm NIR seems to require specialty and/or professionally licensed equipment to obtain. It's no where to be found, from what I can see. So it appears I'm unable to begin fully utilizing the Catabolic signaling that dwells beyond 660nm Deep Red and 880nm NIR, unless I'm able to get it from direct sunlight during mornings and evenings. And that's not always possible for me.

Hello all!
I am very happy to finally be here and participating in the community.

I tend to keep to myself, or "lurking in the shadows" collecting information and learning without being noticed. I'm not one to join groups or collectives, a bit of a lone-wolf so-to-speak. I'm not much of a follower either, which has landed me into trouble/difficulty from elementary school into the work-place.

I tend to be very analytical, hesitant to trust and one to notice patterns and peculiar details that others don't. The bare-naked truth has been a huge priority to me in my life.

I have watched Uncle Jack's podcasts over the last couple of years, and found Alexis Cowan along the way. It is quite funny when synchronistic events link up... I came here because of the quantum biology and my love and awe of the human body/biology, but have always been super-fond and a student of ancient history, the occult and esoteric.

To hear/see all of my "favourite" subject matters in life all come together in these discourses is amazing, everything from biology, to history, to astrology, etc. AND without all of the "new age" woo too. I have to say I feel a little vindicated because I have been connecting dots for years, and labeled conspiratorial, angry or wasting my time with all of this information. Looking forward to deepening my knowledge. Thank you.

# Thread: Hello and Question About Blue Light Blocking After Cataract Surgery
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-and-question-about-blue-light-blocking-after-cataract-surgery.29724/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 1
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### CyGuy — 2024-10-31T18:28:42+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-and-question-about-blue-light-blocking-after-cataract-surgery.29724/post-341800>

Hello, I am new to the forum starting today, and I have a question.

I had cataract surgery in both eyes in early 2021. I am still in the process of verifying, but I am pretty sure I had the "standard" intraocular lenses with UV and blue light protection. As I understand it, red light balances blue light. I have to work on the computer for my profession. I already have blue screen blockers on my monitor, and I wear blue light blocking glasses. I have a red light on when working on the computer. If my lenses have blue light blocking plus the additional screen blockers cited, is it ever possible that I could be blocking too much blue light to be out of balance with the red?

**Posts:** 6

### GAK — 2024-11-11T06:05:20+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/treating-fuchs-dystrophy.29779/post-342192>

Hello to all from the beautiful Cumberland Plateau here in East Tennessee!
First and foremost I would like to express a huge Thank You to Dr. Kruse and supporting staff for allowing me the great privilege of being a member of this forum. Have been a proponent of "Decentralized Medicine" for decades, just didn't know what it was called. I was recently introduced to Dr. Kruse's work and was blown away by it. Seems like I had been thinking along the same lines for years, but couldn't get my low dopamine friends, family, and colleagues to have any of it.

I have been diagnosed with Fuchs' dystrophy. [https://www.cornea.org/Learning-Center/Conditions-Research-Areas/Fuchs-Dystrophy.aspx](https://www.cornea.org/Learning-Center/Conditions-Research-Areas/Fuchs-Dystrophy.aspx)

Big medicine is telling me the only treatment for this condition is to undergo a partial corneal transplant known as Decemet’s Membrane Endothelial Keratoplasty (DMEK), [https://www.cornea.org/Learning-Cen...nea-Transplants/Endothelial-Keratoplasty.aspx](https://www.cornea.org/Learning-Center/Treatment-Options/Cornea-Transplants/Endothelial-Keratoplasty.aspx)

Have been considering this treatment BUT, as I say often these days, if everything else is a lie, what makes this the truth?

What are the ramifications of introducing unknown donor cells into my "pure blood" body?

Which types of unknowns could be luring in those endothelial cells, what with the health emergency of recent.

It's very hard to find any unbiased information these days, especially with the far reaching censorship we endure today.
I would appreciate any and all weigh ins from the forum members. Perhaps even from Dr. Kruse, God willing. Many thanks! Greg

Hosea 4:6 Common English Bible
"My people are destroyed from lack of knowledge".

### GAK — 2024-11-11T06:07:58+0200

### Magpie — 2024-11-11T22:08:37+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/treating-fuchs-dystrophy.29779/post-342218>

Your best option would be optimising light water and magnetism. My mother has Fuchs as did her husband. She has mild macular degeneration and is at high risk for retinal tears and detachments. Also cataracts which are almost ripe. You can have Fuchs for a long time and require only conservative management. My stepdad died of a trauma aged 80 and never needed surgery for his Fuch's. He loved gardening and did so shirtless and was very brown. My mother is now 82 and no active management of her Fuch's has been suggested.

I remember reading up on Fuch's after my step dad was diagnosed back in 2001. There was only a small entry on Fuch's in the massive ophthalmology text book I read in the local eye ward. It was less than a page. A hairdresser mum went to some years ago had had the transplant so some people do have surgery young.

I suggest you spend some time on Google or DuckDuckGo and find Cell tower info from Europe where towers are banned from being close to schools etc. AND in some countries young children are not allowed cell phone BY LAW.
I believe even in the US cell towers are not allowed close to fire stations because of the affect they were having on the firemen. Lots of info out there.

# Thread: 13 year old injured in a car accident
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/13-year-old-injured-in-a-car-accident.29834/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 14
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### Bridgette1 — 2024-11-19T00:26:59+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/13-year-old-injured-in-a-car-accident.29834/post-342601>

Hi everyone,
I'm Bridgette from Darwin, Australia. Our precious 13 year old was the innocent victim in a horrific car accident on the 12th January 2024.
We were told to switch the machines off many times but we refused. She survived the first 6 days with so many injuries and flown to another state for life saving surgery where we stayed, my husband and I separated from our son for 8 months.

Her pelvis was shattered, so many many broken bones, punctured lungs she lost her leg which kills me...

She has a _diffuse axonal_ injury and had several cranial operations - she now has a titanium plate on one side, no occipital bone (it was crushed), her right side of her body (including her face) (her dominant side is weak) her right eye is damaged and she can't see well (and her right eye doesn't blink) and her left ear (hearing is damaged) she had ruptured bowels. These are just the main injuries.

I had been using red light therapy for many years and as soon as we were out of ICU (after 52 days) we used the red light in her own room and took her outside as often as we could. I also used music/frequency, we refused the toxic hospital food and cooked and sourced the best foods for her to recover. As soon as she could swallow we provided fish oils - l-threonate - lions maine - high doses of vitamin c - homeopathics from one of only two traditional homeopaths in Australia. We massaged her daily - I've done osteopathy, accupuncture.

She wanted to be home for her birthday in September and she made it. Such a brave determined girl with such a positive outlook. We have been told many times she is a miracle. The Neuro surgeon who saved her life (well there were a few people working on her that day) nearly fell off his chair when he saw her walk into his office back home.

_I am looking at ways to heal her in the next phase_ \- her **nerves**, she is walking with a prosthetic but her gait needs a lot of improvement and her right side weakness (including her face) has improved but she finds it hard to drink still with her mouth and her speech is not the same as the ganglia has been damaged.

Her **mental fatigue** and

Also her stomach - after the stomach operations and all the drugs she was on is not the same and she has an **upset stomach** frequently. I'm trying to find ways to heal including pre biotics and pro biotics, juices. Any other suggestions?

The medical system isn't offering much more than OT, speech and Physio. Any other suggestions would be really appreciated.

I'm hoping to at some stage be able to speak with Dr Jack Kruse to see what his views are on the next phase of her recovery but we are not in a position yet.
Thank you.

# Thread: New From Missouri
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/new-from-missouri.29886/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 1
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### PopSickle — 2024-11-27T15:48:46+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/new-from-missouri.29886/post-342974>

I used to live in Shalimar, Florida before moving back to Missouri (USA).

I got diagnosed with Psoriatic Arthritis the summer after graduating high school in 1984. I started taking naproxen sodium at that time to mange the pain. I eventually added methotrexate, hydroxychloroquine, sulfasalazine, and Humira to my regimen, and added Rheumatoid Arthritis to the mix somewhere around 2020. I was diagnosed with high blood pressure around 2005 and went on Valsartan. Around 2020, I started a thyroid med because my doctor wanted my levels just a little higher than they were.

This year, I moved to Missouri and had to get a new doctor. He went to school in Russia and I thought he might have had an education that was disconnected from Big Pharma. He said if my cholesterol levels were above 100, he'd insist on putting me on a statin. I said I wouldn't take them. When my labs came back and I was at 92, he still wanted to put me on a statin. Seems he likes the kickbacks from Big Pharma. That, and the fact that I couldn't get in to see a rheumatologist for six months to continue getting prescriptions, made me want to get off of all my medications.

My kids started on a modified keto diet (one is a type 1 diabetic, so it made sense) and just to get me off of the fence, I went on it. Just doing that has allowed me to eliminate all my prescriptions without a significant increase in pain, although I do move a little slower. My intention was to investigate the Whals protocol for its anti-inflammatory effects to see if it helps, and then I found this forum.

That brings me to now. Hi, everyone!

Greetings all,

Newbie here, coming to you from Colorado in the U.S. I've been following JK for a while now and I am intrigued with his positions. Likely for the same reasons most of you are.

As someone who rarely joins forums on anything of substance, I wanted to take a moment to say hello, extend the proverbial olive branch, and expand my horizons of knowledge.
**To be clear, I am joining the Forum with an objective in mind.** Two actually. If either resonate with you, the following story will not be "TLDR". If the title alone doesn't capture your attention, no worries. I hope you find what you are seeking.

That said, if I connect with one person who shares a common experience as mine, or with someone who I can inspire or who can inspire me to challenge my methods of thinking, "GREAT SUCCESS!" (-Borat)

**About me:**
\-20+ years in the financial industry in Sr. Management. Great money, all the fixings, travel, cars, etc. I had an epiphany along the way and left the industry for sake of mind, body, and soul.

(Why does someone leave a mid 6 fig job without a safety net in place? Ask me and I'll tell you. Hint, it has to do with centralized industry. I assume I will find camaraderie here.)

\-All previous health indicators (centralized medicine's indicators, e.g., BP, Chol, Diet, BMI, exercise, etc.) were/are within good to excellent range.

\-Recently suffered a bout of long Covid (6+ months of pure exhaustion and poor lung/circulatory function) which I believe led to prolonged extreme inflammation (of which I also believe) that led to sudden bouts of gout and eventually, a stroke. In that order and with no history of medical issues, EVER. No meds, no flu or flu shots, rare cold (every few years). No allergies. You get the picture.

\-Mentally and physically, I felt like S\*@T **ALL** the time. Yes, I probably drank too many craft beers, so sue me  And, I think you will agree, that is likely not the culprit of reason #1 I am joining this forum.

**Reason #1 for joining the Forum**

**I had an ischemic stroke at 46 YOA** (Warning - centralized explanation here): Full loss of motor function on the left side. After IV brain and heart catheter surgeries (I won't call them minimally invasive as I can already hear Dr. K saying "MAXIMALLY INVASSIVE"!!) I have since regained 99% motor function and cognition and am faring very well. In fact, better than most. For that, I am eternally thankful.

Not one doctor can tell me why I got a blood clot however they can tell my why it led to the stroke. Is that actually helpful going forward, NO. **I want to know WHY?**

**Reason # 2 for joining the Forum**

To date, I feel "better", but not "healthy" (low energy & brain fog from before the stroke still remain) although I am in even better shape (appearance wise) than I was before the stroke.

I need to formulate a new strategy since my medical team's answer is making me a lifetime customer of big Pharma. (Statins for someone with low BP? Blood thinners for an active person with no history of any cardio or neuro issues? **These medications? For life? It just doesn't "feel" right.**

Lastly, this is more than anything, a newly invigorated pursuit of truth, justice, and knowledge. If I can get an ounce of each, I will be better off and can pass it along to those I care about.

Thank you advance and I look forward to whatever comes next.....

~TR

Agree with comments above, regardless of the lag time it's the most likely precipitating factor.
As for any predisposing factors the usual suspects apply- lack of sunlight and poor circadian habits, frequent air travel, cumulative and ongoing EMF exposure, accumulated deuterium, booze, cigs, other shit in our environment and water, previous vaccines/abx/meds, pre-conception/maternal health - tick any and all that apply. Even if you didn't have a PFO (which is v unlucky in this context), the DVT would probably have travelled to your lungs instead and caused a PE. I'm hoping your docs at least checked you for the rare coagulation disorders some young people have.

JK has written a lot on this- be worth having a read. A mid-western doctor on substack has also written a lot on this including damaged zeta potential following the jabs- could be worth a look as well.

### Anthony Smith — 2024-12-26T20:30:58+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/coming-to-el-salvador.30021/post-344368>

If you stay in Atami or Shalpa you will meet many Mito’s on the beach at dawn.
I found most locals do not speak English but are happy and helpful with communications. A language app is an often used tool to bridge the gap.
Jack travels a lot so may or not be there at that time. Even if he is the odds of running into him are remote. My understanding is he does most (all) his consults over the phone/internet even with people who are in ES. Just so you know.

### boerekamp — 2024-12-30T18:17:59+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/new-member-as-of-today.30032/post-344484>

Hi All,
Let me shortly introduction myself:
I am born and raised in The Netherlands.
Studied Chemical Engineering at the Technical University Eindhoven.
Specialization Material Science.
Worked for Philips Electronics (&Lumileds) in The Netherlands and Germany for almost 30 years in several R&D and production facilities mainly in Ceramic materials, Glass and Metals:
1\. Soft magnetic material development (ferrites) used in inductors
2\. Sintered Bioceramics (HOAp) for implants
3\. Glass and glass to metal seals for Incandescent, Fluorescent lighting, High pressure sodium SON and CDM. a.o.
4\. Fluorescent materials for Energy saving lamps and LED lighting.
5\. Scintillator materials for Medical Systems, CT, PET and SPECT.

Retired a few years ago and currently mainly working in and around my residence, my vegetable garden and perennial garden.
Furthermore I like to ride my off road bike

That's it for now,
Rgds, Jack

### friendlyBrownCat — 2025-01-06T15:54:19+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/new-gold-member-from-cold-wi-usa.30051/post-344778>

Webinar i found about labs = [https://optimalklubs.com/about-labs-webinar/](https://optimalklubs.com/about-labs-webinar/)

Summary of labs follows, I am checking other podcasts and will update as i see more detail. Also perhaps someone might add more detal around ranges for tests if known.
Another detailed post on this seems to be here: [https://jackkruse.com/what-are-the-optimizing-labs/](https://jackkruse.com/what-are-the-optimizing-labs/)

### **. Comprehensive Lab Panels**​

-   **Description**: Dr. Cruz describes using a wide-ranging initial panel to gather a comprehensive health picture. Over time, he has narrowed this to a core set of labs addressing most health issues (90–95%) while reserving "zebra labs" for unique cases like biotoxin illness.
-   **Optimum Ranges**: Not provided.
-   **Relevant Detail**: Labs are part of a holistic health assessment and must be interpreted alongside family history, symptoms, epigenetics, and lifestyle factors. Labs are compared to paint on a canvas, helping to create a picture of health. He does not specify what labs are Comprehensive panels but i am looking in other places. Based on my research it usually means:
-   Code:

    ```
    Complete Blood Count (CBC): Evaluates overall blood health, including red and white blood cells, hemoglobin, and platelets.
    Comprehensive Metabolic Panel (CMP): Assesses organ function (liver, kidneys), blood sugar, electrolytes, and proteins.
    Lipid Profile: Measures cholesterol levels, including HDL, LDL, and triglycerides.
    Thyroid Function Tests: Includes TSH and sometimes free T3/T4 to evaluate thyroid health.
    Vitamin and Mineral Levels: Often includes Vitamin D, B12, and iron panels.
    Inflammatory Markers: Such as C-reactive protein (CRP) or erythrocyte sedimentation rate (ESR).
    Hormonal Panels: Such as sex hormones (estrogen, testosterone), cortisol, or insulin.
    Infection or Immune Markers: Sometimes panels include tests for specific infections or immune function
    ```

    .

* * *

### **2\. Highly Sensitive CRP (C-Reactive Protein)**​

-   **Purpose**: Measures systemic inflammation.
-   **Optimum Range**: CRP values should ideally be **very low**, such as **<0.5**.
-   **Relevant Detail**:
    -   CRP is described as a key marker of inflammation, which Dr. Cruz frames as the foundation of disease.
    -   Inflammation is likened to a "house fire," with CRP acting as the "lighter."
    -   He highlights the importance of CRP in understanding cellular signaling disruptions.

* * *

### **3\. Vitamin D**​

-   **Purpose**: Monitors immune system health.
-   **Optimum Range**: Not explicitly provided.
-   **Relevant Detail**:
    -   Vitamin D levels indicate whether the body has enough "firefighters" to manage inflammation effectively.
    -   Dr. Cruz links Vitamin D deficiency to immune system dysfunction and notes its importance in seasonal testing (e.g., addressing low levels in the fall).

* * *

### **4\. DHA (Docosahexaenoic Acid)**​

-   **Purpose**: Reflects metabolic efficiency, sleep quality, and gut health.
-   **Optimum Range**: Suggested range is **60–701** (based on lab reference values), with abnormal levels such as **\>120** associated with gut and sleep issues.
-   **Relevant Detail**:
    -   DHA is central to the hormone chain and provides insights into overall hormonal health.
    -   Elevated DHA suggests specific issues like poor sleep or gut dysfunction, which can impact metabolic efficiency.

* * *

### **5\. TSH (Thyroid Stimulating Hormone)**​

-   **Purpose**: Evaluates thyroid function.
-   **Optimum Range**: Dr. Cruz suggests **0.5–1.0** as optimal, which is narrower and lower than the standard medical range of **0.5–4.5**.
-   **Relevant Detail**:
    -   He links TSH to symptoms like low energy, libido issues, and eyebrow thinning, even when levels are technically "normal" by standard ranges.
    -   This narrower range aligns with his emphasis on addressing subtle dysfunctions.

* * *

### **6\. Cholesterol Panel**​

-   **Tests Included**: LDL, HDL, Triglycerides, CRP.
-   **Purpose**: Interprets cardiovascular health.
-   **Optimum Ranges**:
    -   **CRP**: Low, ideally **<0.5**.
    -   **LDL**: No specific target provided; context matters more than the absolute value.
    -   **HDL**: Higher levels are preferred for a healthier lipid profile.
    -   **Triglycerides**: Lower levels are favored.
-   **Relevant Detail**:
    -   He frames LDL cholesterol as part of the body's natural healing response during inflammation or acute illness.
    -   Emphasizes inflammation (CRP) over LDL as the key cardiovascular risk factor.

* * *

### **7\. Quarterly Lab Monitoring**​

-   **Purpose**: Helps patients track health trends over time.
-   **Frequency**: Every quarter for 12–18 months.
-   **Relevant Detail**:
    -   Patients should learn to correlate lab trends with how they feel at different values, building a "library" of personal health data.

* * *

### **8\. Seasonal Testing**​

-   **Purpose**: Addresses seasonal health challenges (e.g., vitamin D levels in fall).
-   **Relevant Detail**:
    -   Dr. Cruz mentions using cold exposure to address seasonal drops in free T3 levels and their associated symptoms.

* * *

### **9\. Paleo FX "Cheap Dirty Paleo Hack"**​

-   **Tests Included**:
    1.  Highly Sensitive CRP
    2.  Vitamin D
    3.  DHA
-   **Purpose**: Provides a quick and cost-effective snapshot of systemic health for generally healthy individuals.
-   **Relevant Detail**:
    -   He emphasizes that these three markers together provide valuable insights into inflammation, immune health, and metabolic function.

* * *

### **10\. Estrogen-Progesterone Ratio**​

-   **Purpose**: Evaluates hormonal balance, particularly in women.
-   **Optimum Range**: Not specified.
-   **Relevant Detail**:
    -   Many women have "upside-down" ratios, which can lead to health issues.
    -   The ratio serves as a guide for treatment decisions but is not elaborated on in detail.

My wife and I used to have a house in Panama City Beach, FL in the panhandle. Our community was Carillon Beach Resort. It has some nice homes but the panhandle in general is cold in February, and it's off season. So, you can expect some places to be closed or have limited hours that time of year. You'd be better off if you kept driving and got to the gulf coast.

Since you seem healthy (huge caveat - disease requires radical change), just take it one day at a time. The "red pill" is a lot to swallow. Don't do anything super rash. Take a vacation, get your eyes and skin in sunlight for a while before really meditating and pondering on the next steps. You don't want to make big decisions in Wisconsin in winter, your cognitive tracts aren't at their best. There are varying levels of steps you can take.

Just as an example, I live and work at the 41st latitude, nearly in Oregon. So, my light sucks! BUT, I live on the coast with zero population density and can embrace the weather as it is, since the average winter's day is about 50 degrees. Cold plunging, surfing, working outside all day without a shirt on are all accessible to me still, which helps a ton vs a place like Wisconsin in winter. Currently, my wife and I are still too busy as young physicians to spend too much time in the tropics, so we bought a place in Todos Santos, an hour north of Cabo. This is by far the easiest, fastest and cheapest place for us to fly to get our redox fix for 4 weeks or so over winter.

I believe building this mitigation strategy while you figure out life is critical. You start to recognize what "better" feels like and can chase it while still achieving financial, professional, parenting, etc goals.

Just $0.02

Hey Tom,
If there is a way to open the window, I'd do that - or get outside for 20min or so for the sunrise. See if you can have sessions outside (meetings, phone calls, breaks etc). That should be the main source - as you know.
I'd use the panel to also flood the room with red, to compensate for the blue from the screens etc. Just have it somewhere that it's not interrupting the work you do. I'm currently on night shift (in Australia) I use it behind me to offset the screens.
Then try a morning and evening session in front of it with as bare skin as possible. They should have come with eye protection so you don't look directly into it.

# Thread: From rubber duckie to black swan mitochondriac

### Carly18 — 2025-01-05T17:48:45+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/from-rubber-duckie-to-black-swan-mitochondriac.30062/post-344742>

Please try again later.", "lightbox\_start\_slideshow": "Start slideshow", "lightbox\_stop\_slideshow": "Stop slideshow", "lightbox\_full\_screen": "Full screen", "lightbox\_thumbnails": "Thumbnails", "lightbox\_download": "Download", "lightbox\_share": "Share", "lightbox\_zoom": "Zoom", "lightbox\_new\_window": "New window", "lightbox\_toggle\_sidebar": "Toggle sidebar" }

Hello everyone!
I’d like to introduce myself as I sit in the dark, lit by candles at my kitchen table. My name is Carly and I live at the 53N latitude in Alberta Canada. I’m on the cusp of selling my home from which I’ve lived and worked for the past 11 years, raising my son and trying to find ways to stay out of the meat grinder healthscare system here. I’m a registered massage therapist, completely disillusioned with my industry and the direction it’s trying to take even though I love helping people manage or get out of pain.
I discovered Dr Kruse while I was trying to figure out why my kid wouldn’t sleep and my hair was falling out 2 years ago. His podcast with Rick and Andrew FINALLY made the pieces fit because I knew there was something else that was making all of us sick and it wasn’t just stress, “inflammation”, junk food or lack of pHARMaceuticals.
In 2023 I introduced red light therapy (technically Nov 2022), sunrise viewing, grounding and sun maxing and discovered that summer that I could actually be in the sun all day and not burn or feel uncomfortable. This past year I really committed to being outside as much as possible with the least amount of clothing I could handle, have kept my home completely dark after sunset and before sunrise, use bb glasses if I have to be around ALAN at night and am embracing cold plunging. I’m also no longer a no coiner thanks to Dr Cowan (and Sam Parker) and her Bootcamp Reboot classes. She’s such an incredible teacher with a HUGE heart.
I’m still struggling with some health issues and have decided it’s time to commit to renovate my redox by diving in head first.
I’m just getting to know how to navigate this forum and I’ll try my best to read as much as I can and learn how to be even more of a savage. I’m scared of leaving my family behind in this country but I also want to provide a legacy for my son, turn back my clock and get some skin in the game. I’m not going to be that rubber duck in the middle of the pacific anymore.

# Thread: Hello Everyone
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-everyone.30114/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 6
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### Jackson K — 2025-01-15T05:28:48+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-everyone.30114/post-345217>

**Hello everyone,**

I’m new here and wanted to share my journey and some of the struggles I’ve been dealing with. I’ve been a tech abuser for the past eight years, constantly in front of a screen—whether it’s my phone, computer, or TV. I played basketball and soccer in high school and have always been involved in athletics since I was young. These days, with college and my job, I’m on screens for 8+ hours a day, which I now realize has likely taken a toll on my health.

### **My Health Background**​

-   I’ve had **two varicocelectomies** that I deeply regret and wish I’d never done.
-   I had my **tonsils removed at age 5.**
-   This past June, I had a **lip laceration** and, unfortunately, got a tetanus shot despite my reservations. I haven’t taken any other vaccines since the ones I was “required” to get as a child. (No COVID vaccine for me—nice try, Fauci
-   I have **minor tinnitus** in my right ear from a gunshot.
-   I experience **floaters and BFEP** (Blue Field Entoptic Phenomenon).
-   I’ve had **three migraines**: two with aura and one without, all triggered by stress or excessive screentime.
-   **Poor posture** has always been an issue for me.

### **What Triggered It All**​

I’ve always struggled with stress and anxiety, but things got significantly worse last November. I suffered a panic attack at a dermatology appointment while getting moles removed. That night, I came down with a fever and chills, and I woke up with my heart racing, having another panic attack.

Since that day, I’ve had severe anxiety, and panic attacks because of the increase in visual symptoms I was experiencing. A week or two later, I had an ocular migraine, which made everything worse. Since then, I’ve experienced:

-   **Visual snow**: A mild graininess, especially in dim or dark lighting.
-   **Excessive BFEP** and **floaters**.
-   **Afterimages**, **starbursts**, **halos**, and **glare**, especially noticeable at night.
-   **Tinnitus** louder than ever before.
-   **Tension headaches** that come and go.
-   **Brain fog**, **low energy**, and **low libido**.
-   **Sore, tense eyes** and a **tense neck**.
-   **Heavy exercise** temporarily worsening symptoms.
-   ****Depersonalization****

I visited an ophthalmologist who confirmed that my vision is now 20/15 (improved from 20/20) and that my eyes are healthy. He suggested that my symptoms could be related to stress and anxiety, but there was nothing he could do aside from referring me to a neuro-ophthalmologist. After reading up on these issues, I realized that conventional doctors don’t have many solutions for this, so I decided to go the decentralized route.

### **Current Progress**​

Since then, my anxiety, stress, and symptoms have improved. My tinnitus, headaches, and even some of the visual disturbances have calmed down. I still deal with floaters, BFEP, glare, halos, starbursts, afterimages, and mild visual snow. I’ve learned that stress and anxiety make everything worse, so I’ve been focusing on keeping those in check.

Luckily, I live in a rural suburban area, so I’m not surrounded by excessive RF or EMF exposure. Here’s what I’ve been implementing so far:

-   **Cold Thermogenesis (CT).**
-   Religiously wearing **blue light-blocking glasses** when using screens or indoors.
-   Seeing the **sunrise** and grounding daily.
-   Using **red light therapy.**
-   Eating more **salmon** and other foods rich in DHA.
-   Limiting screentime and using **f.lux** on my devices.
-   Drinking a lot more water.
-   Doing **light exercise** and **neck stretches** to reduce tension.
-   Regulating and mitigating **nnEMF** in my bedroom and workspace.
-   Practicing **yoga** (I’ve always been into it and can even do the splits, but I’ve been doing it more consistently now).

### **Looking Ahead**​

I feel like I’ve torn my body down from years of stress, anxiety, screens, and EMFs. But since implementing these protocols inspired by Jack’s work, I already feel better. I know I still have a long way to go, but I’m optimistic about the progress I’ve made so far.

If anyone has suggestions or advice based on your own experiences, I’d love to hear them. Thanks for reading!

### js92014 — 2025-01-23T05:35:54+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/new-from-tiny-parkville-mo.30157/post-345612>

Hello fellow truth seekers!
I guess I will start at the beginning, seems like a logical place. I am Jerry, I am a consumer commodity relocation specialist- a class A professional driver for a global LTL company. My wife is an RN, currently working from home in a hospice leadership position. She has also done infusion work, but went back to hospice because that's what she loves. We have 3 kids- boys, all boys... all three born in May and 8 years apart. We have MY 24 year old, HER 16 year old and OUR 8 year old. We just built our dream home FULL of LED lights- ugh! My wife has several ailments, mainly migraines. Anyone here who themselves suffers from them or has a loved one who does knows how painful it is to watch someone you love hurt and you're helpless. Of course doctors just want to poison her with meds. Several years ago we found the migraine food list, and number one on it was onions which we ate a ton of. Armed with that list and our new paleo/gluten free diet we have managed to cut her migraine frequency way down. Now, were not perfect... we have had a hard time sticking to gluten free because some of the alternatives are terrible- but we try. We get all our meat fresh from a friend who raises them free range grain/antibiotic free. We are a seafood family to a degree, my wife can't have shellfish because of the histimines in it cause migraines (or so we've read years ago). We eat a lot of salmon, but I know its not wild caught- we will shop better for this from now on. We do not consume any raw meat, poultry or seafood. There are other fish types we eat as well, no tilapia ever as we heard its an engineered fish. We try to shop farmers markets for produce, but that's tough this time of year. We do not cook from boxes or by way of a microwave, all of our meals are prepared at home using fresh (as possible) ingredients with no or few items with any preservatives. We make our own chili, spaghetti, fajita, and jerky seasonings as every one in the store contains preservatives. We get no vaccines and our 8 year old has not ever had a shot in his life. His pediatrician told us not to bring him back after he was born unless we we're going to let him poison our child. I guess this is a good time to say that due to my wife working from home she also home schools our youngest. Our two older boys have had very minimal vaccines in their younger years, and NO FAUCI OUCHY for any of us.

Two weeks ago I heard a snippet of Dr. Jack Kruse on a podcast, it was about a 15 minute cut. That was all I needed to head out on a broad search for more. I was delighted to find lots of podcasts on Rumble and Spotify, which made me extremely happy because those are two platforms I subscribe to. I am not a fan of social media at all. Anyway, I started listening and 2 hours went to 4 went to days and days now. I have largely given up trying to talk to anyone anymore about health or politics, its generally a complete waste of my time. However, I am passing on links to Dr. Kruse videos and podcasts and its truly catching on. We are die hard conservatives and I never thought anyone would drag me away from my political podcasts- until now.

We are eager to start this process, and we think were at a good jumping off point because of the years of paleo and gluten free practice. I am REALLY wanting to start light therapy on all of us, and get screen protectors for our devices. I have done many hours of research awaiting approval to access these forums, but am very excited to communicate with good folks who have long started this particular therapy. I have not spent a dime as of yet because I've no idea where to begin, and finding anything in the 380-400NM rating is nearly impossible. I am finding lots of stuff in the 600 plus up to about 960, but nothing higher either. I know more than one podcast I listened to Dr. Kruse mentions the importance of both 380 and 1000. Some of these lights are very, very pricey and I don't want to buy without knowing the prescription for each wavelength- distance from the light, need full body or no, how long of exposure, which wavelengths require eye protection, etc. I am more interested in lighting that can be easily moved versus installing one, so my wife can easily move it about the house as she works, teaches, cooks etc. Reversing the affects of blue light is something we can easily do now, then we can move on to refining diet, increasing sun exposure, waking for sunrise, and other regimens as we learn from this community.

So- this is us.

I would like to thank everyone in advance for any advice on lighting and screen protectors that you all recommend, I assure you that you won't be wasting your time as I will begin buying immediately. We look forward to a long and healthy future right here! I apologize in advance for the length of my intro and I hope I didn't violate any TOS in posting it.
