Hi everyone! My name is Michael. I just joined the forum today, but have been following Jack's work for the past year. I am 35 years old and have lived in Costa Rica for the past 7 years with my wife. Both my children (5) and (1) were born here.

I have been completely fascinated by Jack's work and all the understanding it has brought me. I have always loved Costa Rica from the beginning, but when asked why I love it so much, I couldn't always provide a clear answer. Now its obvious, the light and the light stability. I have always just felt better here.

My education background is as a mechanical engineer, but for the last 10 years I have worked in the health and wellness sector. I have been apprenticing with a tribe of botanists called the Ingano located in the southern region of the Colombian Amazon, studying how plants can be used to treat illness and disease. Tech detox, circadian alignment and sunlight have always been a part of my protocol for my clients, but I never quite understood why it worked. I just knew it did in fact work.

Now, thanks to Jack, I am beginning to understand why my methods have been successful. Even better, I'm leaning more into these aspects to strengthen my work with plants. I frequently work with the sacred plants more traditionally associated with Amazonian cultures, in the methods that were taught to me by my indigenous teachers. I have found that meshing all of this together in the perfect container can result in a state of radiant well-being.

I am not struggling with any disease myself, but I arrived here on behalf of a loved one. My father-in-law was diagnosed with ALS about 7 months ago, and this situation has left me feeling like all my tools weren’t enough, pushing me to search for something deeper. This is what has brought me here and to Jack. I am seeking more knowledge and understanding so that I can help him in whatever way I can.

He is from Canada. He claims his symptoms started as much as 4-5 years ago when he looks back on it now, small things adding up over time. Only recently did it get to the point where his regular physician referred him to a neurologist who made the diagnosis 7 months ago. His life was one of shift work, fluorescent lighting, and very few sunrises.

Now, I finally was able to convince him to move down here to Costa Rica with us. He is staying in a house down the road from us, has no Wi-Fi in the house, turned his cellphone off last month and hasn't touched it or any technology since then. He sees every sunrise and sunset, and lights are off by 7pm. We are 1 month into this protocol, and the symptoms haven't yet slowed down, but I am hopeful. He has committed to keep this protocol for at least another 3 months before he wants to return home to visit his family, so I hope we can make some progress.

Anyhow, that is a little about me and why I am here. My hope is to learn and understand more so I can help others and spread the word, as well as helping my father-in-law. I seek wisdom, and Jack has already offered so much. I'm still hungry though.

Pura vida my new tribe.
\-Michael

If you have an iPhone, there are settings you can tweak to make the screen red. It is laid out here somewhere in the forum.

# Thread: The water  Boy
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/the-water-boy.30333/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 8
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### Bobby Boucher — 2025-02-22T09:12:52+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/the-water-boy.30333/post-347106>

Hi everyone
I am and always will be controversial on all subjects you will either agree or disagree but I will always give you a hug and respect your disagreement ,so let’s start about me I try to stay anonymous to the General public due to the censorship I endured in 2020 to mainly protect my young family (I was a late baby starter) after the authorities were visiting my residence frequently so i required a more robust strategy I managed to hold my account on Twitter just I had multiple short term bans all through 2020/2025 and still to this day red flagged on X and account restricted I called out the covid bullshit at the same time as Mike Yeadon except he has a much larger following I’m only a minnow I started life in engineering specifically hydraulics fluid dynamics and thermal dynamics and spent 23 years in this field what an amazing experience travelling the Globe to all corners. I hit my early fourties’ and had some sort of mid life crisis ditched my wife at the time and changed careers into something completely different I chose to go into the field of Distilling and Fermentation processes I had two choices back to university or go somewhere obscure and learn from experienced individuals in that specific discipline so I signed up for Uni and proceeded after my first week I quickly learned I made the wrong choice I was learning with kids who were kind of taking the piss of me and a lot of the mathematics I had already done previously in engineering so I changed strategy and got a huge break I managed to get a unpaid kind of apprenticeship on an island on the west coast of Scotland with a huge profound Name in the Industry he took a chance with me and gave me a step on the ladder (which I will be be eternally grateful forever for at that juncture in my life I was completely broken and felt rejected) I started at the bottom of the process and worked 18-20 hours every day for one year learning from very old individuals and wrote all my learnings in my new black book the art of fermentation and Distillation I learned and was humbled to learn from amazing characters I was summoned one day into the Big Boss office and was sat down and he said to me where and what do you want to do in this industry I told him straight and within 1 week I had secured an interview at one of the oldest distilleries in Scotland the rest is now history hope you enjoyed my introduction I gave you an insight to my life as I never do ,I prefer to stay private and in the shadows and fight against tyranny and Evil from the back benches I accidentally came across Dr Kruse on you tube Ted talk in 2011 I think can’t remember exactly he struck some kind of cord with me ,then about 2 years ago he appeared on Ahmad Malik podcast who I support and talked to once on the phone I think he wanted me to go on his supporter stories which I refused as I would loose my Job and my pension which I worked bloody hard for and I only have 1-2 years left before retirement so that’s a tiny part of who I am I have been working with water half my life and other liquids and gained unparalleled knowledge and if I can help in any way within your group . ” you will never get what you want until you are grateful for what you have.” ❤️

### Base_Strength — 2025-02-25T02:18:26+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/barbell-strength-coach-coming-on-board.30345/post-347258>

Greetings, decentralized savages! This is my kind of group.

I’m a barbell strength coach from the Austin Texas area who’s been doing cold thermogenesis and grounding for over a decade. I knew morning sun set my circadian clock, but I didn’t grasp the full science or how it jacks up mitochondria and hormones until now.

I’m here to learn everything I can. A week ago, I started weaving sunlight into my lifting days. I throw open the garage doors, no matter the temp, and let natural light flood in. Between sets, 4 to 6 minutes rest, I step outside, stand in the sun, and hold a green leaf to ground. It’s already boosting recovery and firing me up for the next set. Or maybe it's in my head but I do feel like something is happening here.

Can’t wait to dig deeper with everyone!

Leave it to Western psychology to tell you your grieving "abnormally." The truth seems to come at a price as well. I used to be super emotional. A feely kind of person. Now if I feel it’s anger. But not like a rage or emotional anger. More like looking at the 70% that got it who still to this day think they did the right thing..,I see them as a bunch of dumbass idiot brainwashed fools that brought back the word retarded (that we all decided to stop saying because it was rude) and yet there is not really another word for it. They aremt developmentally disabled. They just chopped their own balls off and handed them over to Fauci and Gates on a silver platter. Do I still love my siblings and friends who got jabbed and also shamed ME for not doing so? Yes. But do I also think they are dumbasses? Yes. And am I angry that I can’t say anything without being gaslit? Yes. But I’ve stopped giving a shit because it’s pointless. And guess what? My self-confidence is higher than it’s ever been in my entire life. Because I let people judge me and fought with them about being right my whole life and now I KNOW I was right and that THEY are the idiots. Not me. I don’t need their validation. I suppose I have been pretty damaged since birth, so maybe this only applies to the people born broken. But right now I am thriving for the first time in my life.

So that is motivating me. Find what motivates you

# Thread: Hello All, New Member here

**Posts:** 1

### ShawnH — 2025-02-28T19:54:59+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-all-new-member-here.30380/post-347596>

I am excited to be here and to learn more from Dr. Kruse and the members of this forum. I've been fascinated by and studying light for over the past decade. This recent fascination was sparked due to my research in the cannabis space and trying to reproduce the solar spectrum for indoor growing. I researched the
Emerson effect (Red+Far Red/NIR) and different light spectrums effects on growth and photosynthesis and worked with lighting companies to implement extended spectrums (outside of PAR). During this time I had an innate belief that we also harvested energy from the sun as humans though I didn't understand the mechanisms of action. Here are some photos of grow rooms I designed in 2017 using far red and near IR.

For the past 30 years I have been interested in and studied the human body, initially as a performance athlete and coach, but as the decades ticked by, my focus became general heath and then longevity.

I only came across Dr Kruse this past year and I have found him to be the most genuine and intelligent person that I have come across. I have learned more from him than any other doctor or researcher that I have studied. I came across him on the Danny Jones Podcast, it was the first time I had ever listened to Danny Jones or Dr Kruse. That podcast sent me down a rabbit hole that I have been digging into ever since. Cheers!

# Thread: Hello from the SF Bay Area
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-from-the-sf-bay-area.30482/>

### AlbertW — 2025-03-14T23:34:15+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-from-the-sf-bay-area.30482/post-348609>

I live in Palo Alto, CA and work remotely as a software engineer.

I haven't had serious health issues (that I know of), but I do have moderate myopia and sleep apnea and have experienced chronic fatigue for 10-20+ years now. My kids also have some chronic health issues, so I'm trying to research health in my spare time.

A few years ago, I started optimizing via diet and exercise, but it wasn't until recently that I learned about nnEMFs and sunlight from Jack and others on X. I really subscribe to Jack's theories, though I have to say that his delivery is often a bit harsh. I totally subscribe to the theories that "nature knows best" and people evolved for real reasons. Everything in life (e.g. technology) is a tradeoff and there are rarely free lunches. I must say that I feel like an outsider in the tech community with my beliefs.

I've been working from my backyard using an rCLD monitor all day recently, trying to maximize UV + IR and hopefully improve my myopia this way.

I'm also looking to move to a new town/city in the US and build a custom EMF fortress house. Any recommendations? Unfortunately, I have a lot of requirements:
\- love California weather (I know I'll need to compromise here). not too hot. not too cold. hate humidity (mold?)
\- avoid states with vaccine mandates for school
\- don't want to live on flat land in the middle of nowhere with no connection to society. should be at least within 20-45 minutes of society
\- have a decently good public or private school nearby in case I don't have time to homeschool

I have to stay in the US for work. Any suggestions?

### AlbertW — 2025-04-05T00:25:09+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-from-the-sf-bay-area.30482/post-350115>

I had a Building Biologist come out with the 200Mhz-8Ghz and 20-40 GHz meters and didn't seem to pick up too much RF nearby (likely 4G only, though need to verify). I heard a fixed-high-pitched sound indicating cell, but the RF was in the 50-250 uW/m2 range, which isn't ideal but also isn't sky-high. In some rooms in my house, with WiFi off, I can achieve 0-10 uW/m2, which seems decent for sleeping.

Yesterday was our first day of having the entire family sleeping in the basement with those breakers off. Body voltage 5-20 mV range (grounding via outlet ground). RF 0-10 uW/m2, < 0.2 mG. Seems as close to perfect as you can get for Bay Area, I'd think, right? The 2 toddlers still kept waking up at night, so no immediate changes. I'm hoping that this is just a healing process and they won't recover immediately.

We also started giving the toddlers DDW and more salt. More grounding, getting sun outside.

Considering buying a Magnetico. Would it help in my situation?

One concern I have is that body voltage (compared to outlet ground) is 400-800 mV just walking around my first floor (even when I'm not close to walls). I'll need to do a test to turn off all breakers to the house, but I wonder if I'm picking up electric fields from wiring for ceiling lights in the basement. I also heard that DE radiates a lot farther from walls than the 60 Hz signal. I saw 200-800 mV readings with a Greenwave EMI meter. My neighbor has solar, so maybe it's from that? Maybe I need to do a 10-minute consult with Anthony.

I don't live near downtown PA nor Stanford fortunately, to avoid the bulk of the 5G.

Nevertheless, I am planning to spend a month or two soon in ES at Jack's recommendation to see if my son's eczema, irritability, and anaphylactic reactions can clear up.

### jweiler — 2025-03-15T22:08:06+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-there-new-member.30488/post-348689>

I'm glad to be part of this forum. I recently watched Jack on the Danny Jones show and was blown away by all the stuff he talked about there.

I would say I feel fairly healthy but I've been a software developer for the last 12 years and didn't realize how dangerous all the blue light exposure is (and nnEMF). I have used [https://justgetflux.com/](https://justgetflux.com/) some in the past but found out about [https://iristech.co/](https://iristech.co/) on this forum and have been using that now. I also started switching light bulbs in our house to incandescent.

Also, I have worn contact lenses for the last 15 years and they have UV blocking on them. I started making sure I get morning sunlight without my contacts or glasses on. I also made an appointment to try on some non UV blocking contact lenses, but I don't know if that is better or worse than glasses? I'm pretty sure my current glasses block UV light.

All the info is a bit overwhelming, but I do love spending time in the sun and with the days getting longer here in Pennsylvania I should be able to do more of that.

For many years I was focused on finding the right supplements and the right food to keep me healthy. Too know that circadian biology is vital to being healthy is a new idea for me, but it is a freeing one. While it's not necessarily easy the concept is super simple. I just need to work at doing the right things.

Anyway I'm excited to keep going through the blogs and forums posts to learn more.

### Marshall_Sponder — 2025-03-22T19:13:01+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/istanbul-restaurants-i-liked-for-jack.30535/post-349132>

## As promised from the February Member's call (and March)​

## Sultan Mehmet Restaurant & Cafe​

[Sultan Mehmet Restaurant & Cafe - Google Search](https://g.co/kgs/mqbfA5S)

Cankurtaran, Alemdar Cd. 18/A, 34122 Fatih/İstanbul, Türkiye

This is near the Archeological Museum, worth seeing, and a nice park nearby, most of the historic stuff is in the same area in the old city.

## Rumeli Cafe & Restaurant​

[Rumeli Cafe & Restaurant - Google Search](https://g.co/kgs/QrUaunU)

Akşemsettin, Fevzi Paşa Cd. No:13, 34080 Fatih/İstanbul, Türkiye

Near everything downtown, including Bazaar.

There was another restaurant where we had breakfast the first day but I wasn't able to locate its exact location from my bank statements.

# Thread: From artificial glow to natural radiance
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/from-artificial-glow-to-natural-radiance.30766/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 4
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### riksa — 2025-04-26T15:03:00+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/from-artificial-glow-to-natural-radiance.30766/post-351315>

Hello from the 60th northern latitude. I go by the name Matias.

It was light that pulled me from the darkness. I was on multiple heavy psychiatric medications without actual pathology, living and sleeping next to the elephants foot. My nights were illuminated by the high powered LED street lamp. Eating gutter oil for breakfast, smoking cigarettes made out of store receipt papers when I ran out of real papers. I was effectively lobotomized and doomed for an early demise. But I liked the sun, so I spent a lot of time in the summer outside. And this one summer, in an instant some switch flipped inside me for no apparent reason, that I must rebuke all of that. Stop all medications immediately, which I do not recommend, and became healthy. I believe it was the sun that gave me just enough clarity to see. Or God.

Took me two years to recover subjectively, with tremendous anguish and suffering. I was doing everything I can to become truly healthy. Peeling the layers month by month. Going from exercise and macros to supplements and fasting to cold exposure and nutritional composition nuance and so forth. Then I saw a video on Youtube. It was uncle Jack. Talking a bunch of crazy stuff with supreme confidence.. I've seen this before -- another false-guru. But there is something here. Then he starts to talk about light, blue light. And it triggered some animous compulsion inside me, because it matched a hundred precent what I've personally noticed of the effect of blue light. That made me watch and dig more and more and slowly my mind expanded. It was the light again that pulled me in.

I have had a fully strict light discipline for this year. Every morning when I get up I go straight to the forest for an walk for an hour. Bare head, bare chest and nasty looks from elders passing by in the -5C weather. This has truly recovered my self. Not just my health, but my self. I'm curious, now my curiosity runs so rampant that I constantly have to run to the computer to check some thesis out. My engines are purring again. I admit, I would have not figured this out by my self. I was 23 in the first passage, now turning 27.

I want to give thanks to you, Jack.

### riksa — 2025-04-26T16:12:25+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/from-artificial-glow-to-natural-radiance.30766/post-351316>

At the beginning, I slept with my head 15cm away from an mobile-data Wifi router. In a nnEMF hellhole. Coincidentally, one of the psychiatric medications prescribed to me was Gabapentin. Now why is that note worthy? Gabapentin acts on the voltage-gated calcium channels. By blocking it. The probable mechanism of action of the RF frequencies(Pall, 2018) by which it causes damage. It was prescribed for anxiety, and non-surprisingly, I had to take a high dose for it to work, and it did. Now, when I moved apartments and reduced the EMF to non existent levels as to that, the gabapentin works now _stronger with **15%** of the dose.

Edit: I don't believe in coincidences. It was one of the only medications I had to upkeep after the turning point, now I realize for a good reason._

# Thread: Introduction: Daniel, Seeker of Truth, Health, and Wealth
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/introduction-daniel-seeker-of-truth-health-and-wealth.30830/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 1
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### Nitton76 — 2025-05-04T16:59:09+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/introduction-daniel-seeker-of-truth-health-and-wealth.30830/post-351889>

**Greetings, Kruse community!** I’m Daniel, a fervent seeker of truth, health, and wealth, and I’m profoundly honored to join this exceptional forum, inspired by your audacious, paradigm-shifting discussions. Your deep dives into biological optimization, fearless questioning of mainstream narratives, and commitment to thriving through nature’s truths have compelled me to craft this introduction—a candid, expansive exploration of my journey through health struggles, relentless truth-seeking, and a visionary drive to empower humanity. This is a comprehensive narrative of who I am, why I’m here, and how I aspire to contribute to our shared mission of living with unparalleled vitality. If my story resonates, I invite you to read to the end and join me in forging connections to spark transformative ideas that can reshape our world. Full transparency: I’ve spent the last 90 minutes collaborating with AI to craft this message. While AI shaped the words, this is unequivocally my voice, my heart, my message.

**How I Found Kruse’s Work**
My journey to Kruse began in December 2024, ignited by an encounter with Robert Breedlove in Mexico, shortly after their podcast interview. Robert’s infectious passion for Kruse’s insights—circadian rhythms, light as a therapeutic force, and ancestral health—seized my attention, propelling me to immerse myself in Epi-paleo Rx and the podcast. Initially, the book seemed like an echo of my existing practices; I was already dedicated to natural light exposure and sleep hygiene. But I live by the ethos, “I don’t do anything that ain’t worth overdoing.” 2 weeks ago, I escalated my morning and evening routines to an extreme—uncompromising sunrise exposure, grounding barefoot on grass, and a strict ban on evening screens, post 5pm. The impact was profound: my energy soared, my focus sharpened, and I rediscovered a vitality dormant for years. My wife, grappling with mental well-being challenges and hormone imbalances managed by pharmaceuticals, has seen progress with these changes—her sleep is improving, her mood is lifting—but we both face a long road ahead. This transformation is a clarion call, and I’m here to deepen my understanding with your collective expertise.

**Health: Extreme Routines, Real Food, and Mental Struggles**
Health is the bedrock of my existence—without it, all else falters. My physical health is formidable, and my appearance reflects years of disciplined care, but my mental capacity falls short of my peak a decade ago, when I thrived in the frenetic chaos of emergency management. Back then, my brain was a dynamo, wired for rapid, multitasking decisions—crisis mode was my forte. Today, my work is strategic and long-term, building ventures like Cowbolt and FYSIGO, requiring sustained focus and discipline that often clash with my brain’s current wiring, exacerbated by health challenges. I’ve always possessed an extraordinary capacity to work, performing at levels that mask my struggles from others—most wouldn’t suspect anything’s wrong. Yet, I know there’s a vast reservoir of untapped potential within me, waiting to be unleashed if I can optimize my brain. Only three months ago did I realize I’d been grinding for years—five, perhaps eight—immersed in client work with global giants, pushing without pause. Recent changes are steering me in the right direction, but I’m far from my full capacity.

Overtraining was and is my Achilles’ heel; every 6-10 months, I’d pursue grueling workouts, chasing performance, only to crash with burnout or injuries. Fitness trackers provided heart rate variability data, but I ignored my body’s signals, driven by an insatiable need to excel. Years of poor sleep cloaked my mind in fog, blunting my cognitive edge. I’m unvaccinated, a choice rooted in my unyielding commitment to individual sovereignty—a principle I’d defend to the end.

Eight weeks ago, Epi-paleo Rx catalyzed a revolution, pushing me to amplify my morning and evening routines to an extreme: sunrise walks without sunglasses, grounding on dew-soaked grass, and a complete halt to blue light after dusk. This approach has worked wonders—my sleep is restorative, and my mental sharpness is slicing through tasks, though not yet at my decade-ago zenith.

At the same time, the past two months have been demanding. I rely on ADHD medications a few days a week to sharpen my focus for critical tasks—strategy sessions, pitches, deep work. I’m adamantly opposed to pharmaceuticals; they’re a crutch that clashes with my principles, and I resent their necessity. Once or twice a month, when creativity eludes me, I’ll take an 8-centiliter gin and tonic, always early morning, never after 2 PM to safeguard my sleep. The creativity boost can be the edge I need to deliver on commitments, but I’m not proud of it—I want to thrive without these aids. My goal is to eliminate both entirely, and I’m relying on this community’s expertise for natural alternatives—circadian optimizations, dietary adjustments, or biohacks to rewire my brain. More concerning are symptoms possibly linked to a stroke or poor brain blood flow: tingling in my limbs, occasional brain fog, and sluggish thoughts, flagged as bad blood flow to parts of the brain on the scan.

Recent sleep improvements have reduced fog and tingles, but I remain worried and am eager for Kruse-inspired strategies, such as mitochondrial enhancement or vascular health optimization.

I’ve been using LiveO2 contrast therapy ([https://liveo2.com](https://liveo2.com)), and it’s proving transformative. Its Adaptive Contrast technology—cycling oxygen-rich and oxygen-depleted air during HIIT exercise—feels like it’s supercharging my circulation, flooding my brain with oxygen, and boosting energy, directly supporting my goals for mental clarity and blood flow.

My blood markers are exceptional, though some doctors raise concerns about my 350+ cholesterol levels. Holistic practitioners would likely endorse my overall data, reflecting a body in balance. I’d never consume the processed junk Liquid supports our customers to produce. I source raw, unprocessed A2 cow dairy and meat from an Amish farm or Wild Idea Buffalo—their bison is phenomenal, you’ve got to try it!

**Truth: Courage in the Face of Dogma**
Truth is my guiding star—a dogged pursuit of unfiltered facts, no matter how controversial. I’m inspired by those who sacrifice to speak out, staking their reputations, careers, or livelihoods for what’s right. During the COVID-19 turmoil, Dr. Mary Talley Bowden was a lighthouse, suspended from Houston Methodist Hospital for championing early treatments like ivermectin and challenging vaccine mandates, prioritizing patients over institutional pressures. Anders Tegnell, Sweden’s state epidemiologist, was another pillar, standing resolute with a data-driven, no-lockdown approach that defied global hysteria. His response to a reporter’s query—“The whole world is wondering which data you are using”—is my all-time favorite quote: “The question you should be asking is what is the rest of the world using because I haven’t seen any data at all.” That piercing clarity crystallized my commitment to grounding every belief in rigorous evidence.

My own truth-seeking led me to an Israeli study demonstrating natural immunity’s superiority, with a 6.72 times lower reinfection risk compared to vaccination, reinforcing my unvaccinated stance and spurring deeper research into immunity. In business, I embodied this truth: one of my CEOs departed when I refused a vaccine mandate, a decision rooted in my unshakeable belief in individual sovereignty. This wasn’t merely a stand—it was an expression of my core identity. I’m always open to those who risk everything to share their message, and I bring that same openness to this community, eager to engage with your perspectives, challenge my assumptions, and build on data-driven insights that pierce the veil of misinformation.

Health and Wealth: From Industry Contradictions to Freedom’s Horizon
Health is the bedrock of my life’s mission, and I’m building FYSIGO, a decentralized health marketplace to empower individuals with tools for wellness. I’d never touch the processed liquid foods Liquid supports—I call them “poison” for a reason, and I stand by that conviction. For 19 years, I’ve led Liquid, one of the world’s few specialists assisting global giants in producing the sugary drinks and processed junk I believe are undermining our health. The irony is sharp; this work has sustained my livelihood and continues to do so, but it contradicts my values. I built Oatly’s first U.S. factory, amplifying their “poisonous sugar water,” and if asked to build another, I’d do it—business is my reality—but I’d proclaim their products’ harm from every platform. Truth is non-negotiable, even when it’s tied to my income. Wealth, to me, is freedom—self-sufficiency and providing for my family, not merely financial gain. Bitcoin revolutionized my perspective in 2018, unveiling decentralization as the path to true empowerment. Now, Cowbolt.com is my top priority, transforming Bitcoin into a practical, everyday currency for peer-to-peer transactions—splitting bills, sharing meals, or settling group expenses—using Bitcoin, Liquid Bitcoin, and Tether on the Liquid Network. It’s private, non-custodial, and fosters freer communities, enabling people to onboard friends and family through real-world utility, not speculation. I’m calling on Bitcoiners to join as Founding Partners to shape this mission, building a financial system that supports health, sovereignty, and freedom. Cowbolt and FYSIGO embody the ethos of seizing control, breaking free from restrictive systems, and forging a future where health and autonomy prevail. I don’t need to work—I choose to, because I love it, just as I loved the adrenaline of emergency management. Yet, my current strategic work demands a mental capacity I’m striving to reclaim, making sleep and cognitive clarity paramount.

**My Mantra: Truth, Health, Wealth**
“Truth, health, wealth” is my daily compass, anchoring me amidst a sea of noise. Truth demands unfiltered facts, no matter the cost or controversy. Health fuels vitality, empowering me to pursue my mission with unrelenting drive. Wealth unlocks freedom to live authentically and support those I cherish. Their order is deliberate—prioritizing money over well-being or honesty leads to imbalance.

**Current Focus: Unleashing Mental Capacity for Global Impact**
I’m here to sharpen my mental effort, the critical lever to unlock my vast, untapped potential when time and physical effort are stretched to their limits. My formula—Results = Time × Physical Effort × Mental Effort²—reveals that clarity, focus, and strategy are the true catalysts for transformative impact. I’m channeling this into Cowbolt.com, liberating people financially to prioritize health by making Bitcoin a seamless, everyday currency, and FYSIGO, cultivating wellness communities grounded in biological truths like circadian alignment, nutrient-dense nutrition, and mitochondrial vitality. My current strategic work—unlike the crisis-driven emergency management of my past—clashes with my brain’s wiring, particularly given my health challenges, making enhanced sleep performance and cognitive capacity non-negotiable. I choose this work because I love it, driven by passion just as I was in my crisis management days, but I’m desperate to elevate my life and unleash the full potential I know lies within me.

**Let’s Connect**
If you’ve journeyed through this entire post, you’re my kind of truth-seeker—thank you for staying with me! I’m here to learn, share, and contribute to our shared mission of living better through biology. Want to dive deeper? Find me on LinkedIn (http://www.linkedin.com/in/daniel₿) for updates on Cowbolt.com and FYSIGO, and my reflections on truth, health, and wealth. I’m passionate about meeting new people, so reach out for a FaceTime or Zoom to brainstorm health, truth, or world-changing ideas. Thank you for inspiring this introduction—let’s uncover the truth and build a brighter future together!

From Florida With Love!
Daniel

# Thread: Hello ALL!
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-all.30833/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 5
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### BradyMartinik — 2025-05-05T03:48:34+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-all.30833/post-351910>

Hey everybody,

My name is Brady Martinik. I just turned 19 a little over a week ago and I currently reside in suburban Northford, Connecticut, USA. My health journey started out after COVID when all my environmental polluters caught up to my young mitochondria and I was left obese, sad and hungry to feel how a wild human should. I grew up labeled a “Talented and Gifted” child, within Rockefeller’s indoctrination camp and traditional schooling came very easy to me. I loved the appraisal from parents, peers, teachers, family and friends. A prospectively good slave in training, ripe to spin the wheels of the NGO’s ideal paradigm. I loved sports, hockey, lacrosse, baseball, football, tag, bikes, it didn’t really matter, I’m always up for a competition.

However, some of my earliest memories are my parents growing frustrated. Frustrated with my inquisitive mind. Always asking ”Why?” Or “How?”, never satisfied, sticking my nose into any conversation, task, trial and tribulation I could weasel my way into (Frequently averse to the liking of whom I’d relentlessly question. ). It arose to the point that they’d submit a question cooldown. Precisely at this time I received my first digital device and these devices never grew tired of me. Access to the internet and an infinite library of videos, games, and answers to my questions never ceased! I grew very fond of these devices but kept a natural balance due to my mind, body and spirits intuitive love for activity and REAL dopamine that my body craved just the same. This teetering of the seesaw hadn’t shot me in to the sky or slammed me on my ass yet… But surely, as you can presume, in due time, it did, which I’ll get into later.

Fast forward to middle school and everyone else was getting bigger, taller, stronger, but I lulled behind. Deemed a late bloomer, everyone else growing in height and bicep peaks, and me waist circumference and weight. Staying up late nights on bright blue lit devices, gulping down glyphosate, corn syrup and a laundry list of other toxins from big box foods religiously, culminating a slow but steady trek toward low dopamine device dependence just to stimulate a fleeting spark to continue on. I can remember my first thoughts of ending my suffering, not deep rumination, not imminent, but an overcast whisper that shadowed my mind being lit up by blue light from a tablet, or DS in the darkness of night. Still social, still making my parents proud with A’s in school, still playing the sports I do dearly loved, but dragging along instead of fiercely attacking life with vigor and vibrance as Nature permits.

Around this time as well, 7th-8th grade, 2018-2019, kids began to talk about masturbation. “What is this I thought?” A flex of pride and masculinity at the time. Encapsulating these conversations is a vivid memory of a lunch table conversation “Some kid told me on Xbox that he never masturbated in his life and he’s a junior in high school!” \*The table bust out laughing.\* “Seriously!?” “What a loser!” I chimed, trying to protect my image of pride and masculinity myself. I had never masturbated a day in my life, didn’t even know what It was or even had the testosterone too due to the circumstances I described. But with my handy dandy device my questions were answered. Every website I came across answered the same. .Org .Edu .Com .NIH .MED had all said the same. “Masturbation and Pornography are healthy and normal and should be experimented with!” So, I obviously followed suit to the digital GOD, how could I not! All signs pointed forward. Explicit, vivid, graphic imagery, a SWORD of dopamine in my pocket any and every time I desired.

Fast forward again, January 2020, 8TH Grade, my friends and I began to experiment with extremely high THC street marijuana carts and again I followed the crowd. Another dopamine sword in my armory. A week after my first time smoking marijuana we got sent home from school indefinitely for a little virus called the “Coronavirus”. Amazing! No school! Just me and an internet connection. The pornography and masturbation lie relatively dormant and in control, a weekly or monthly thing. Marijuana became a weekly endulgement as well. Smoking weed and stuffing our faces with pizza, cookies and cakes, and funny movies, filled with the thrill of hiding out secret from our unknowing parents was the weekly routine with my buddies and I. My dopamine receptors melting with delight. An innocent endulgement. Yet the devil seethed at the path to come, as I traversed mindlessly down this unknown dark road. I felt guilty about smoking, lying to my parents, masturbating, but it wasn’t out of hand just yet. Still dragging along.

During this time I became immersed in a virtual no restriction, no filtration, world of gaming as well. My parents resisted the excessive gaming but I tied their hands claiming that It was a socialization aspect as we were locked down still due to the control experiment we now called the “COVID” pandemic. 12 Hours Daily I endulged in this digital world. Playing video games, bonding with others from 13-25 doing the same things as me, gaming, smoking weed, masturbating, ALL in more and more excess slowly but steadily as I attempted to fill the endless dopamine void unknowingly. I competed in gaming competitions and treated it like a job, streaming on twitch, making YouTube videos, playing wagers (Let’s throw in a gambling addiction and the stimulus of bank deposits and transactions larger than I he ever seen before while we’re in this dark dopamine storm while we’re at it right?), new weaponized content machines like TikTok, YouTube Shorts and Instagram Reels, High Defintion Pornography, etc, being optimized at Light speed, in order to fuel this global dopamine fire. I was the moth to the flame. Burning my hands on this piping stove repeatedly, numb to it’s burning sensation.

Fast forward again, 2 or 3 years this time. This storm approached MACH 10 and I became insufferable. Whenever I stepped out of my room, looked in the mirror, etc, I was ANGRY, depressed, less and less social, less and less active, less and less pleasant, the mask and facade I was able to upkeep out of the virtual world was too small to shelter what I had become. My health and spirit slipping away before my eyes. One day my parents called me into the living room and showed me my pictures from my hockey portraits and told me they couldn’t send these out to any family members. I was broken. I stormed away and balled. I couldn’t stand to look myself in the mirror but with the confrontation of my parents I knew I wasn’t hiding my reality from anyone or anything, any more. It was real, it was here, and it had to be dealt with. That overcast shadow of hopelessness and the eternal escape of death engulfed my soul now.

Nevertheless, my soul’s flame although diminished, lay eternal, with hot embers burning in my core. The very weapon that insidiously and mercilessly tormented me would be my tool. The light in the darkness was there I just had to access it. I used the internet now to fuel and educate myself on how I could fix what I had destroyed. Not a little boy anymore, no one there to save me but me, I did what I had to do, slowly, still these demons slithering and striking me at the onset of any weakness of my spirit, I fought and I fought and I fought for my indomitable spirit and birthright back.

As I weaponized my mind with knowledge about these demons, asked “Why?”, asked “How?” and asked “What?” I could do to fix myself these addictive dopaminergic pathways I was coerced into were weaponized against the Evil dark paradigm with the very Evil they used to do so. They didn’t realize it but they had just battle hardened and weaponized their worst nightmare. The coin they carved was flipped and now I sit here typing this message with a Fire in my Soul that will Light up an Army. An army of hungry, broken, corrupted, violated spirits the same as me. Tirelessly searching for the fuel to the embers of their hearts that won’t fleet. That fuel is the sun. I know their tricks, I know who they are, and I know their game inside and out.

I am here now for all the little boys and girls doomed to drown in the darkness I was swallowed by for so long. Every day I grow increasingly and exponentially more and more aware of the mechanisms used by the controllers that tainted my soul and consciousness. Stripping away, piece by piece, with every sunrise and sunset, the lead these Evil, transhumanist, globalist, technocratic, pieces of plastic. Hello, all you wonderful people! I will spare you the story of my upbringing, as I'm sure it will sound like any other kids' born around the turn of the 20th century. i.e late nights with video games, highly processed foods and drinks, slow degradation of any and all ambitions, etc.
What I do think is important and what I hope some of you may relate to or even find inspiration in, is the point at which I turned it all around.
I was 19, homesteading in the high plains of Colorado. Life was good, until it wasn't. The land I had spent a year and a half living and working on was made no longer available me to. I was told to leave, and that was that. I now had a choice to make, return to my life of toxicity or answer the call that has been echoing in my heart ever since childhood. So, with my dog and what little belongings I had, I set out to find the truth, to be with Nature in a way I had so long been yearning for.
Fast forward 6 years and I am still walking that same path, still searching for my tribe. Whether I have found it or not will be determined by the response I get to this post. But regardless of that, I will be eternally grateful to Uncle Jack for giving me hope and speaking truth.

### Mat.I — 2025-05-19T08:43:20+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/i-am-a-noob.30881/post-352878>

Just a few suggestions -
Mitigate all nn-emf to acceptable levels as per SBM 2015 (attached)

Make sure your wife is getting the morning sunrise (feet on ground) , lots of grounding etc. As much sun as possible (as per Jack's protocols).
Stay dark once the sun goes down (no ALAN what so ever). Use candles or very low lux red lights if you need something.

If you understand DSMO and you are diluting it correctly - you can apply it with intention e.g. brain stem exit ~ Occiput, C1 - C3 region, Spine + sacrum, Abdomen, carotid + radial artery. You could also pair this briefly with NIR light per zone. Do your own research and do not do this every day as this should be cycled... 2 to 3 days per week max..

Digestive bitters may help before meals.

Try castor oil packs over abdomen / liver area before bed.

For the vagus tone rebuild - gargle/hum after meals, & cold facial baths, ice pack side of neck / behind ears

As much grounding as possible.

Up DHA I would aim for at least 3g per day.

Have daily fermented foods (go easy at first if not use to them). e.g. kimchi, sauerkraut, kefir other fermented veg etc.

Focus on electron dense foods - seafood (oysters), pastured fatty beef, pastured eggs, bone marrow, bone broths, offal (liver, heart etc), cook with tallow. I would get rid of the carbs/grains etc.. I take it you cannot afford DDW at this stage so create your own. Stick to mainly protein and plenty of fat with ferments added. When / if you have normal veg cook well and pair with plenty of fat e.g. ghee or butter

\* watch out with the methyl doners as they can oxidise - do not do these everyday (do your own research) if you continue these only use a few times a week and make sure they are taken on days when outside and grounded. Do not push these hard if you decide to keep using them.

Try some meditation in the day along with use of 40Hz gamma frequencies (in am) + 10Hz alpha-theata border after sunset

Low dose (not more than 1mg) melatonin can be really helpful for this situation (do your own research)

Research Li orotate

Gait + rotation walking would be good for vestibular-occular reflexes and cerebellar brain stem coupling etc..

Elbow to knee taps for brainstem - spinal loop

Humming + palate taping (for vagus and crainial nerve field)

Head hold + diaphram press - reconnects fascia + brainstem + gut clock

Keep up the massages and do it with a clear head and good intentions (preferably grounded) as this helps map the fields

Research and add some light acupressure basic points that would be good are GV20, PC6, KD1, ST36, 3rd eye (Yintang), LI4, GB20. Look at how to close gates off to.

Look for a mobile acupuncturist or someone that will be open to treating her outside in the sun whilst grounded, however make sure you have vetted them as damage can be done to a sensitive system if they do not know what they are doing..

Hope this gives you a few ideas and helps.

All the best

Mat

# Thread: Hi from Sweden.

### GazeofGzon — 2025-05-15T19:53:44+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hi-from-sweden.30909/post-352555>

Hi Guys.

My name is Åsa, this is a old viking name meaning godess, but im no godess, Im just a creative from Sweden the land of extremes, the land with dark winters and little day light and light summers where the sun hardly sets.
I have always been into "health" and my book shelf is filled with all the fad books from food gurus on diets and lifestyle but they never really sat right with me, they just seamed to miss something. now i know better now i know what was missing.
About a year ago i got quite disturbing sensory issues in my body i kinda figured out what that could be directly and instinctivly tossed my shoes off in middle of mid winter February, and upped my saunas and cold plunges. Even before getting a confirmed diagnosis 6 months later i had already got a nice tan lost 15kg and found Dr Jack and read his book and listened to many many podcasts.
Im splitting my weeks between Stockholm and my familys farm. I follow the epi paleo RX prescription and i watched the sunrise every day until now when the sun in freaking Sweden goes up at 4.00 and sets at 9.30 its really the toughest time so far. ( I gladly take advice on that )
One morning not long ago when the sunrise was at 6.00 i had a way to close encounter being chased by a big ass wolf, im not kidding you, it followed me all they way home to the door, things you get to se and experience at sunrise. As a spirit animal crossing your path its supposed to mean to trust your instincts. as I try to do every day in this work as i aiming to heal from this "blipp" with nature and questioning everything everything everything.

Hi Anne (sorry if I have your name wrong!)

So sorry for the delay replying, I have had so much going on lately with the sale of the house, and getting everything ready, as you have heard! We are scrambling around selling everything and organising visa's and somewhere to stay in Panama.

So you heard the punch in the mouth ha ha! We really needed it, I honestly can't tell you how grateful I am to Jack for giving me shit over it, we needed to hear it, we did it just at the right time, and the buyer for our house is so excited to be buying it, sad really when you're awake, knowing what they are buying into.... being a savage says f\*ck it!

So, you will think we are crazy, but we have never been to Panama before! I have been to Dominican a few times and love it there, but I researched lots of countries, obviously visa and residency options for different places and read the forum here and Panama was mentioned a few times. In my 1st ever Q&A, you will remember I asked Jack which place he recommended, he said Panama and gave his reasons. I then did a deep dive into Panama, reached out to David Lam on here and joined Facebook groups for Panama Expats and asked lots of questions. We feel right now that it is going to be the right choice for us, it has got to be better than the UK right now!

The specific areas we are looking at are: Costa Esmeralda, San Carlos, Coronado, and Gorgona. We have spoke to many people in Panama already and have sorted rental accommodation for when we arrive, we are going to spend time in each area until we decide specifically where we want to be. I have already got the attorney placed with all the required documents sent over to them (they have to have the originals to submit the visa paperwork to immigration) but we have emailed scanned copies so they have them to open the file. I do like Coronado, but think that one of the other 3 areas would be a little better for us as a family with them being smaller and a bit quieter. We have seen some properties to buy, but obviously would not commit to anything until we have spent some time there, but we can comfortably buy a property cash and live a pretty good life, giving ourselves 'time'.

In terms of schools, I do like PCIS in Gorgona. There are other schools, but it depends on your own children I think. As my eldest is autistic/ADHD, having him in school in Panama may not work, but we are willing to try it, and if it doesn't work, I will home school him. There are many expat children around the Coronado area that are home schooled. I spoke to a guy from Wales over the phone who moved to Coronado in 2022 and they home school both their boys and love it. There are also groups for the kids that are home schooled so that the kids can get together and at least not lose that social interaction etc. My autistic son was at a specialist school here (near York) and he was served 30 days notice recently as they apparently couldn't meet his needs! Basically they couldn't control him in ways they wanted to, the views he had about immigration, the banks, the state of the country, dimming the sun, cloud seeding, not wearing sunscreen, I could go on... So all we can do regarding schools is play it by ear. The situation regarding schools for us did used to be 1st on the list pretty much, now it is way further down the list, as long as we are out of here and in an area we can add back time, the schools will come, and it will all work out.

We did consider El Salvador, but exactly the same as you on that point, and considering our kids etc, Panama for us is the best option, and all going to plan we should be there in 5/6 weeks

Thank you for your message, it means a lot. We feel so clear about it all, have no concerns and are not nervous about it at all, we can't wait!

Listen to the beginning of that June Q&A again and try and imagine Uncle Jack is saying it to you!

Let me know if there is anything else I can help you with, and again sorry for the late reply

Claire.

### Szen — 2025-06-10T17:23:18+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/a-greeting-from-singapore.31090/post-354429>

Here goes nothing.
Hi, I go by Szen here. Chinese male, will be 32 this year, always resided in Singapore. I was born with transposed heart arteries.

If you keep telling an eager child: "You don't know anything, I'll do it."
The child gets the message: "Someone who knows better will take care of it. I'll only get in the way and be told off."
Amplify that with the "virtue" of meritocracy, and you get a child who never develops self-worth.
He will either seek external validation by trying to hoard the highest scores, or by withdrawing into "anything and everything all of the time". Or both.

At any rate, I'm here to pull myself out of the well that I'd become too afraid and almost too weak to climb out of.
I don't really understand anything right now. What I do know is that I cannot stay in a place where people are free-range chicken in a factory farm.
Certainly not when I can still feel the "side effect" on the left of my ribcage from boosters before my eyes were open to the TV-like static in my vision and ringing in my right ear.

I'm grateful that Uncle Jack has built and maintained a wonderful lighthouse here. I got the message that I should not think of my attempt at error correction as palliative.
The mark of a true greatness is not the ability to use great things, but to turn average into great.

I shall quietly study so that I can ask the right questions.

# Thread: LA to Sweden, health rollercoaster, new to Jack's info
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/la-to-sweden-health-rollercoaster-new-to-jacks-info.31249/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 3
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### emajen — 2025-07-05T21:00:18+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/la-to-sweden-health-rollercoaster-new-to-jacks-info.31249/post-355819>

Hey folks, hey Jack, my name is Seth. I'm a 39 year old dude living in Sweden, married with two small kids. I have been on quite the health journey since I got COVID 4 years ago, and just turned a corner on Jack. Found him through a podcast he did where he tore up some slippery pharma lobbyist, can't remember his name. I thought, I really like this guy, so I started learning more.

The "TLDR": came here to connect and learn more about fixing myself, I have had various health issues which I think are explained by Jack's work.

4 years ago I got COVID, it knocked me down for a couple of weeks but I recovered. About a month later, started having strange health issues and too many symptoms to count. Bone-crushing fatigue, muscle twitches, visual issues, hair loss, PEM just to name a few. Was then diagnosed with long COVID (I have never taken the vaccine by the way, that was a hard pass). After struggling with LC for about 2 years I came across something called TMS (tension myositis syndrome) which explained a lot about what was going on with myself. I used some of the stuff I learned in TMS groups to get better again - well, mostly better.

I consider myself "recovered" from long COVID but I still don't have the same energy envelope as I did before (looking back now, I think I was already going down hill before getting COVID, just kept pushing through), and I just feel much, much older than I really am. Now, just recently, I'm having stomach/gut issues, and I am still occasionally getting symptoms from before. After listening to Jack talk about the 3 pillars (light, magnetism, water, hope I got that right) I started to understand why my body broke down in the first place, and why now. Most of my life I spent living in the sun belt (Florida, Texas and then California), and then moved to the 59th latitude where I was starved of light. I also changed my career to programming, which put me in front of a blue screen all day. I've also been wearing contact lenses since 13, with UV protection. I have unknowingly done everything the wrong way.

The good thing is that I'm stubborn as hell and have always been very driven. So I'm channeling this into changing my life so that I can have more energy to play with my boys and be a better, stronger dad, husband, and human being. I have spent a good portion of my life burning the candle at both ends, used to run 30-40km a week, lift weights, party on the weekends, and work 80 hours a week, etc. But I realize all that stuff was just grinding me down to a nub.

The tough thing is, it's harder than hell to optimize where I'm at, so I need to get smart about it. If anyone's got tips or routines they follow while living up north I'd love to hear it.

Thanks for the community and thank you Jack for all the info you put out there. You've spent a lot of your free time spreading this info and I am so appreciative of that. Eager to learn more.

P.S. I am also big on crypto, forgot to mention, and yes I hold BTC. Was a crypto guy even before Jack, so cheers to that!

### Kathy Spears — 2025-07-05T23:42:01+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/la-to-sweden-health-rollercoaster-new-to-jacks-info.31249/post-355828>

Hi Seth. I relate to your story. I was born and raised in California but ended up in Sweden, married to a Swede. During my 6 years there I was diagnosed with several autoimmune disorders. Eventually I moved back to the states but landed in Tennessee where the lack of sun during the long winters didn't help me at all. I was diagnosed with Juvenile Diabetes within 6 months of being back. Dr Kruse helped me to understand that my years in Sweden set me up for all the autoimmune issues I ended up with. And my move to TN didn't help at all.

It is quite possible that you, too, will not be able to fully regain your health while living at that latitude. If you don't move then at least consider embracing the cold the way the Swedes do. I used to marvel at the way they'd go in the sauna and then roll in the snow! I was always very aware that most of my Swedish friends were very healthy and hearty but they were all outdoors people, regardless of how cold it was. I would try to keep up with them but I remember feeling miserable and not understanding how they could possibly be enjoying themselves. I eventually understood that being very cold helps the body to make the light it is missing. So embrace the suck (as Jack would say) and feel the cold, be uncomfortable! And maybe take frequent trips to the Canary Islands during the long winters.

### emajen — 2025-07-06T21:49:02+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/la-to-sweden-health-rollercoaster-new-to-jacks-info.31249/post-355875>

Hey Kathy, good to hear from you! Very similar story indeed, sorry to hear you went through the autoimmune stuff. It is really, really hard to live here! The weather, the darkness, and I just don't vibe with a lot of the locals.

I would like to move back. We just moved to the country here to get away from the crime, EMF, screens, be closer to nature, lots of things. But I really want to move back to Florida, that's where most of my family is. It would be really hard to do and selling that to my wife would be really difficult, plus with the kids ...I'm in a really tough spot. When I tell my wife about all this stuff I'm learning, I don't think she takes me seriously (or thinks Im crazy, haha) so an uphill battle.

I think "embracing the cold" is what I need to focus on. I have a lake within walking distance for winter plunges. Snow is in no short supply. So I will have to start there. That, and make a mandatory trip for a month or two down south as part of my terms for living here.

Did you get depressed living here as well? I couldn't understand it but about 2 years after getting here I was stricken with such a deep, deep sense of sadness/depression, I have never been like that, and couldn't figure out what the hell was going on. Now, after understanding all this info about light, it's starting to click.

Anyway, thanks again. I hope you are finding the healing you are looking for!

# Thread: Fixing myself to understand how to ultimately breed better racehorses
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/fixing-myself-to-understand-how-to-ultimately-breed-better-racehorses.31276/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 1
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### KStuebs — 2025-07-10T21:47:52+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/fixing-myself-to-understand-how-to-ultimately-breed-better-racehorses.31276/post-356121>

I have Graves' Disease. I was diagnosed in 2007. It has been controlled with trace mineral balance and diet. The information I'm finding here is finally answering a lot of question marks in my mind that apply not just to me, but to my immediate phenotype family members.

I also am a thoroughbred bloodstock consultant/agent. Figuring things out is a passion of mine. I've even researched and written a book as a ghost author about a sensitive topic that finally answered a ton of questions in a highly charged area of political America. Figuring out the Rubik's cube was something I completed at age 12. Figuring out the thoroughbred genetic puzzle to breed top racehorses has been my passion since age 18. I have discovered undeniable patterns in breeding that have allowed my to apply that knowledge for clients to help them breed winners of two Breeders' Cups, multiple Grade 1 races, and many runners with seven-figure earnings.

The new passion is going to be to apply the quantum bio-physics from Dr. Kruse to this art. Horse racing is simply about which horse is the fastest, strongest, healthiest. Thinking about all Dr. Kruse discusses, clearly mitochondrial physics is at play. The things I'm learning have yielded questions that could help learn and direct better breeding and management of racehorses.

For example, heteroplasmy vs. homoplasmy is likely of serious consequence in choosing sires for dams in racing. Clearly there are families that consistently produce top runners (one mare recently producing three Derby horses, and one winner). So many questions come to mind like, does the mitochondria of an embryo become hybridized, damaged, or repaired during gestation. I would assume it does, but looking at the consistencies of some mares over others, what could be happening and when? Also, some stallions make amazing sires, yet offer nothing to the mitochondrial equation, (unless they actually offer some rare influence). Some sires make great broodmare sires, but poor quality sires of runners suggesting that they have strong influence passing on their X chromosome. The patterns of lineage in great horses are consistent, but unexplained. Can these sorts of patterns be an indication of some sort of mitochondrial homoplasmy returning to an offspring, or simple DNA physical genetics? Of course the light equation is something that is a variable more easily controlled that the genetic roll of the dice in breeding two thoroughbreds for a desired result. For example evidence suggests that proper light exposure may be an antidote for respiratory bleeders, with the European yards having far more light in the stalls and yards, versus their American counterparts. Then Dr. K's information discussed that dopamine determines muscle quality, and this has to be yet another serious consideration to the breeding and husbandry choice.

Besides fixing my own health, thoroughbred mating is my passion. I will hopefully develop a proprietary software to collect and apply new knowledge and science. It's just going to take a lot of time and research. BUT, I'm always up for a big challenge!

Love to meet up with you all, chat in person re getting out ot NZ/bitcoin etc.

### Katie P — 2025-07-25T01:26:05+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/washington-dc-mitochondriac-safe-haven-coming-available.31380/post-356927>

Not necessarily looking to meet up, but just wanted to share a rare gem for anyone still weathering the DC swamp. I'm moving out at the end of the summer, and my apartment which is hands down one of the best in the city, is about to hit the rental market.

This place isn’t for everyone. But if you're a DC mitochondriac, this might just be your sanctuary.

Two years ago, I toured over 30 spots before finding this one. I’m no professional building biologist, but I brought my Trifield to every showing, and this was the cleanest I found. Bonus: it’s the _only_ apartment I know of where you can sunbathe _completely naked_ year-round in the middle of Capitol Hill and not get arrested. Yes, really, naked sun bathing in our nation's capital, pretty empowering. This apartment is unique and has a privacy fenced patio and no other building can see it where it is located while the sun makes it apearance all day long.

The insulation? Trash. Which is perfect if you're into cold and heat shock proteins. I run almost entirely without heat or AC. Not just because I’m cheap, but because I know the benefits.

It’s also an older building, so the windows have original glass. There is no modern UV-filtered nonsense distorting your light environment. Natural light floods in.

If you're stuck and trying to do good work here in DC and want a space that supports high dopamine and real biology, this is your spot. Would love to see it go to someone who gets it.

I'm not the landlord, I don't own the property, and my lease is up, so not trying to get out of any contract, but I was just thinking it would be a shame if I couldn't pass this haven onto someone else trying to heal who is otherwise stuck in a toxic environment.

# Thread: What cars are healthiest?
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/what-cars-are-healthiest.31383/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 19
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### bennyhoffman — 2025-07-26T19:28:23+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/what-cars-are-healthiest.31383/post-357009>

Hey everybody,

I’m currently in the market for a new car, and I’m overwhelmed by the options available. There are so many new cars on the market, each with its own unique features and technology. Hybrid engines, full electrical vehicles, new interior display monitors, Wi-Fi/Bluetooth technology and so on.

I’m particularly interested in the possibility of living out of my car for short periods. I’ve considered a 2025 Toyota 4Runner or a 2025 Land Cruiser, both of which have hybrid engines. However, I’m concerned about the potential emissions from hybrids, especially when the car is running. I’m worried that I might be exposed to unwanted EMF while I’m sleeping in the car at night / while driving during the day.

Ideally, I would just be sleeping in the car at night with it off, but I also work and would be driving in the vehicle throughout the day. I’m not sure if I should be concerned about the EMFs from hybrids, or if there’s another way to minimize my exposure.

I’ve read some preliminary research that suggests hybrids don’t produce significantly more EMFs than standard cars, but I’m not sure if that’s accurate. I’m also aware that even non-hybrid cars have a significant EMF problem, so I’m not sure if I’m overthinking it.

I’m open to any advice or guidance. I’m willing to use an EMF meter to test the cars I’m considering, but I need some help understanding what to look for. I also have the EMFSAFE home testing kit, so I’m not afraid to use that as well.

Thanks.

### JacqueAwef — 2025-07-26T23:43:50+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/what-cars-are-healthiest.31383/post-357018>

New vehicles are terrible, avoid them like the plague. Vehicles act like a faraday cage, so avoidance of EMR inside the vehicle is extremely important.

Older gasoline vehicles without bluetooth, wifi, rf cruise control, gps, keyless entry, etc. are a much better and much cheaper option.

The best are old diesel vehicles with mechanical injection pumps, although I realize hardly anyone wants to play that game.
You can remove the alternator and charge the vehicles battery(s) with a solar panel(s) on the roof. As diesel engines don't rely on spark ignition and older models had mechanical injection pumps, the majority of the electrical load is from starting the engine, and once started, the engine needs no electrical power to keep it running.

Probably not the answer you're looking for, but hope this helps!

I've been looking a bit as well. I think you have 2 possible options:

1) buy an old car without all of the electronics (Prob <2010?). Issues will be finding parts.

2) buy a new car, print out the schematics and find a very good mechanic who can subtract the superfluous. Automotive makers are making it tougher to do this, but you'd be surprised how crafty some mechanics are.

### Jessnet3 — 2026-01-13T17:58:10+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/what-cars-are-healthiest.31383/post-365267>

I’m in El Salvador for the winter, but once we return home I’ll share exact measurements. That said, we chose a 2024 Land Rover Defender because it consistently gave us the best readings with our meter - both while driving and when parked. Nothing else we tested came close. Readings were comparable to the ambient levels we see in our 12+ year old Tahoe and even our 1982 Defender. You can shut off Bluetooth and Wi-Fi and it is truly “off,” unlike many other makes (Ford, for example) that continue to emit RF in the background regardless of settings. Like every other modern vehicle it does have eSIM, but unlike other makes it is not continuously broadcasting.

We intentionally selected a baseline configuration without many bells and whistles. Defenders aren’t especially tech-heavy to begin with, but because of that choice, I can’t speak to higher-trim or more optioned models.

### Lisaillames — 2025-07-29T22:10:00+0300

Hello Geeks,
I’m a non geek here to learn, make changes in my health and life and pass on the wisdom to others!
I am 60 years of age, obese, recently gained 40lbs. in less than two years and I want my mitochondria to be healthier and to live a healthier life.
symptoms: fibromyalgia, insomnia, anxiety, migraines, chronic fatigue, pain, shingles outbreaks, sciatica, stiffness in my fingers, brain fog, IBS issues, lack of appetite.
medical history:
Age 60 dx with obesity, chronic fatigue and pain. Age 51 dx IBS and acid reflux. Age 50 dx with fibromyalgia, fatty liver. Age 48 dx migraine, tinnitus, neuropathy in hands and feet, blood clot in the right atrium of the heart due to meta port, pre-diabetes. Age 47 dx breast cancer triple negative BRCA1gene. Age 45 dx interstitial cystitis. Age 30 dx with endometriosis, uterine fibrosis, asthma and allergies put on prednisone, inhalers and antibiotics for about 10 years. Age 21 in 3 car accidents within 3 month period suffered whiplash. Teenage years seasonal allergies, rosacea, acne, heavy bleeding and clots during menstruation. Also, exposed to second hand smoke.
Surgery: age 19 abortion, age 26 removed ovarian cysts, age 30 dx endometriosis, age 47 double mastectomy, age 49 bilateral oophorectomy, age 59 two brain aneurysms.
No covid vaccine
Substance use: no drugs, no alcohol use, never smoked
food allergies: shell fish, eggs
allergies to medications: NSAIDS, acetaminophen, MRI and CAT scan contras, idodine, latex, clorox, penicillin, oxycodin,
current medication: bilanta 90mg, valtrex 3000 mg, naltrexone 4.5mg, amlodipine 5 mg, methocarbamol 500mg, allergic, atorvastatin 40mg, magnesium complex, melatonin 10mg.
supplements: D3 5000mcg, k2 180mcg, zinc100mg
family history:
mother passed away age 54 from metastatic breast cancer
father passed age 29 brain hemorrhage from a car accident
family history on mother’s side: breast and ovarian cancer, diabetes, seizure, bi-polar
After reading many articles of Jack’s I am up watching the sun rise and sunsets, daily swimming in my new salt water pool, outside daily for hours, but I burn in the sun and get shingles outbreaks and migraine, I’m building up my heat tolerance, the tan stays on my body but leaves my face quickly. Wear blue blockers for electronic use, also I have limited my use on electronics, after sunset amber lights only in home. Any info greatly appreciated!!!

### JacqueAwef — 2025-07-30T17:38:55+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-new-member.31400/post-357205>

Great job getting more sunlight and it's fantastic that you did not get the covid shots.

Have you bought any electrical meters to measure for RF/microwaves, AC and magnetic fields, dirty electricity?
Minimizing EMF in your environment is extremely important, much more so than diet or supplementation.

If you still use a cellphone, you will need to reduce your use of it to very few minutes per day.
Anything that uses wifi or bluetooth has to go.

Blue blockers are a band aid for electronics use. I recommend getting a screen that doesn't emit blue light at all.
For example, the daylight computer DC-1, or anything that uses an Eink screen.

The focus needs to be on safe sunlight exposure in a low EMF environment.
Hope this helps!

### Lisaillames — 2025-07-30T20:09:06+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-new-member.31400/post-357217>

### JacqueAwef — 2025-07-30T22:02:43+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-new-member.31400/post-357227>

Some of the most common RF meter manufacturers that I see people use are Cornet, Trifield, and Safe and Sound.
Cornet and Trifield have low sampling rates compared to Safe and Sound and miss a lot of what is actually going on.

Highly recommend the Safe and Sound Pro II as one of your first purchases. It's not cheap, but you get what you pay for. Remember that this meter will only measure radio frequency(RF)/microwaves.

You will need other meters to measure AC electric and AC magnetic fields.
Gigahertz Solutions and Alpha Labs are great manufacturers.

A lot of people will not want to deal with this stuff on their own and hire building biologists to do these measurements for them. That is always an option. I prefer DIY.

### joyfreedom — 2025-08-01T03:39:02+0300

I am relatively new to the Forum and Jacks teachings. I have made changes with greeting the sunrise and sunset, eating more like a great white, reducing the EMF in our home. I am 63 living in New Zealand, I know its not the greatest place for sovereignty and sun. I have started collecting my bitcoin.
We lived in the Gold Coast, Australia for 20 years where my health improved greatly. Now realizing living on the beach and being in the sun was one of the main reasons.
We returned back to NZ around the crazy time of covid, I new instinctively that the jab was wrong on so many levels. I have been working towards to taking my power back from centralized medicine as I had been immersed in it in my younger years. I have never had a mammograms' or smear test. Sadly I did vax my two children.
We have two children and four grandchildren. One grand daughter has Noonan Syndrome, on the lower end of the spectrum thankfully.

I was a very unwell child with pneumonia (collapsed lung) removal of tonsils. Boils and carbuncles. We lived on a farm, which seemed a healthy lifestyle.
When I started menstruating's I formed a ovarian cyst that twisted and became gangrene. From that point on I had problems with more cysts and overshadowed my life from 12 - 40
My mother and grandmother lived to their mid 80's, Mum died from leukemia. Grandmother and mother English, my father is Scotland / English
I'm the youngest of four. My oldest sister and middle sister both died from multiple myeloma, ages 63 and 65. My brother took the jab and it damaged his heart and now he has prostate cancer which he is treating outside the medical system.
The health issues I have now since being back in NZ are tinnitus, shortness of breath when doing any form of cardio. This starting from breathing in the dust from the plant deadly nightshade, it has gotten a lot better but will catch me out at times. I would so love to resolve this issue and my tinnitus. My energy levels are ok now however my recovery time from physical exertion is longer than it should be.
Looking forward to learning more and connecting with over savages

### JacqueAwef — 2025-08-01T17:49:59+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/joys-optimal-journal.31416/post-357333>

One of the best investments you can make is buying a Safe and Sound Pro II.
Then you can start measuring and minimizing your RF/microwave exposure.

I don't recommend using the popular Cornet or Trifield meters for measuring RF/microwaves as they have a low sampling rate. They are cheaper for a reason.

You will also want a meter that can measure AC electric and AC magnetic fields. A lot of options do both in one unit.
I believe Gigahertz Solutions makes some of the best units, but other people have their opinions as well.

Hello all,

I'm a 34 yo SAHM, my husband and I have 4 sons (5, 3, 2, newborn). I am originally from SE Houston, but my husband is from KC, Kansas and this is where we live currently.

I am mainly here because I have not come across someone that was as like minded as we are. We did not vaccinate our children, my husband was not vaccinated, and we did not comply during the lockdowns (we didn't even wear masks/my job didn't know what to do with me and ended up putting me on short term disability for 6 months just to keep me out of the way). We were still impacted by it, as my son was born the day of the first lockdown (we did not have a hospital birth). My family was unable to visit us and it really took a toll on my post partum experience. With that said, we would be foolish to believe something like this will not be repeated within our lifetime, and most certainly our childrens. We were already a family that spent a ton of time outside, but we were not catching sunrises. Since I learned about this major necessity I started doing it right away in Feb (even in the snow) of last year and never looked back (my husband and children began to follow in my footsteps not long after).

My paradigm shift was not in a full podcast, but a podcast clip, Jack said something to the tune in regard to Ray Peat and Weston Price's work, that what they missed entirely was that these tribal groups were eating their food in the sun. It was like I had an immediate epiphany that what I had been sensing about these influencers was right, I just didn't have the missing and obvious piece, which was the sun.

We have been planning to move to El Salvador or Guatemala since last year, before learning about Dr. Jack. I found Dr. Jack through an influencer who I no longer follow. In fact, I was ripped off by her in the new year of 2024. I took a major step back and unfollowed several people and really kept my social media silent for a year. I decided to start listening to Kruse's podcast as I kept being drawn to them. I was hesitant to invest any money into anyone else because I had been ripped off by that influencer. Fast forward to when Kruse defended Dr. Alexis earlier this year, when he did that, I felt again a parallel in our beliefs. I had also came to the realization that influencers pushing certain diets, supplements, and "lifestyles' was stealing precious time and energy. Due to this I decided Alexis and Jack were both worth my time and I am very grateful especially now with everything being a complete disaster with the current administration and feeling more urgency to get moving on our plans to move down south.
