### salva21m — 2025-08-22T04:06:38+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-from-hokkaido-japan.31500/post-358607>

It's getting more difficult to find local food due to the influence of big supermarket chains. As I am in Hokkaido, it is easier to find salmon and other fish from here as a source of DHA. Local meat and lamb also easier to find (I have to try the lamb as it is also big on DHA). I try to avoid carbs, but still when I eat rice or potatoes, I also focus on those from the region. ### DLO — 2025-08-22T04:12:49+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-from-hokkaido-japan.31500/post-358608>

Salmon would not be native to Japan how about sardines or herring?

### salva21m — 2025-08-22T04:40:05+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-from-hokkaido-japan.31500/post-358609>

There are many types of Salmon native to Japan and specially Hokkaido. the region's connection to salmon relates to the Ainu, the indigenous people of Hokkaido. They have a long-standing relationship with salmon, which was a crucial part of their diet and culture. Archaeological evidence from Hokkaido shows that people have been fishing for salmon in the region for nearly 10,000 years. In addition, you also can find the Pacific Herring and Japanese sardines.

### Schneg — 2025-09-06T16:21:16+0300

Hi everyone! I have been a silent lurker for a couple of month now, observing and learning slowly. I found uncle Jack on Spotify in May and since then
I can't stop listening to every podcast I find with him. I always felt something was wrong in this world, but never thought it was THAT bad. Thank you sir for your lifetime work. It is priceless, it's huge and inspiring.

I am a 44-year-old French Canadian and proud to be one of the few who refused the Covid vaccine around here. I never trusted that shit, it felt waaaaaay too suspicious. I was completely stunned to see the majority of people around me complying so easily, without question. I'm used to being a black sheep, but that one was hardcore.

I have few health problems, but enough to feel the need to seek solutions that my doctor seems unable to provide. Since I discovered Uncle Jack, I understand why now! I worked as a chef for 15 years and now as a carpenter/joiner for 6 years. So nutrition and physical health have always been present in my life, but I now understand that there are other, much more important issues. I've read Jack's book and have started reading Power, Sex and Suicide and The Body Electric. I've listened to several dozen hours of podcasts and I'm just starting to get a full picture of the issue. I still have a lot to learn, a lifetime in fact! But I think I've come to the right place to do it.

I started the leptin rx in June and I already see and feel result, it's amazing. I will probably be able to take 2 weeks off this winter and I would love to take the opportunity to visit El Salvador. I don't have a date yet or any specific plans but if you have any suggestions for a time when some of you will be there, I would love to take the opportunity to meet some of you! Since I'm very new to the Bitcoin universe (and because I'm a fucked Canadian), I don't have much money and will be traveling on a tight budget. So I'm open to any suggestions from those who are or have been in my situation.

Thank you uncle Jack for your wisdom and knowledge and thank you everyone for being here and sharing all that stuff.

See ya!
Patrick

### dzmak — 2025-09-09T20:25:54+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/the-spark.31621/post-359336>

I started following Dr Kruse at the beginning of the year. My husband has been listening to reggae style music and played this song for me a while back. I just heard it again last weekend and it took on a much more significant meaning after what I've learned from Dr Kruse.

Just wanted to share because it felt like a summary of everything he has taught me.

## The Spark​

Lennon

Out of absence came the spark
Little flicker just
To start this creation
Waves rolling out
Infinite destinations
Coalesce, come apart
Generation, generation
Simplicity giving rise to
Boundless innovation

What is God?
But a word that people keep on taking for granted
Use it to sow the seeds of hatred that continue getting planted
But the mystery of life is so much bigger than a man's head
No matter how much he inflates it with the worship of the masses
As we segregate life by race, religion, politics, and classes
Illusions holding fast because we're holding to our past
It's time that we look past this
If we're hoping to unite
Recognition
Not the struggle, fuss and fight

From one light, one hum
One endless vibration
Came all life, all love
All manifestation
And our hearts, our minds
All our observations Is all of our existence seeking
Self realization

See the writing on the wall
Let it fall

Boundless innovation...

The Ballad of Samurai Jack
Jack Kruse MD that is.

The movie was wrong; Tom wasn’t the last

The current one sets the bar; for the entire warrior caste.

You can listen to; without feeling you might as well be consigned to hell

And if you can get this man to shine his light your way

Chances are good;

Sick you won’t stay.

Myself I have three mitochondrial/modern life warps

My tv screen and so on gave me cataracts, prostate and what else

The surgeon who put the terminator lenses in bad

Not only blinds me to UV; the repair surgery blinds me with inflammation that remains a drag.

Im going to just go sit in an ice bath; cause unless you can talk to him you can just plus

Hello morning sun; the ground is so dear; ice bath and sauna

Cell phone not near.

If you remain sick

# Thread: New Here, Bronze Member since Sept '23 = Whatsup from Florida!

### MatthewMcKay — 2025-10-20T23:18:06+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/new-here-bronze-member-since-sept-23-whatsup-from-florida.31759/post-361288>

**_Hello_** to my fellow **_Humans_**, I have been a member since Sept 2023 on Patreon but for some reason haven't taken the dive here until today. From looking at the forum topics I can tell that this is the place to connect with true BSMs. I received my BS in Kinesiology, had worked in injury rehab/sports performance post graduation. My current position is Golf Biomechanics & Fitness Professional at PGA Tour Golf Academy, taking advantage of having an outdoor career (though I am aware of the pesticide/chemical aspect of my work environment). I stopped wearing sunscreen September 2023, never wore sunglasses.

It is fun being able to educate my students not only about anatomy, physiology, golf club dynamics & ball flight dynamics, etc but also about the importance of LWM. I work in an industry where dermatologists have scared the shit out of golfers and to avoid the sun..... it is fun going against the grain and getting people to think differently. I am looking forward to meeting more and more BSM thanks for Dr Kruse's burning passion.

_**Uncle Jack got me into Bitcoin**_, which then I reached out and connected with Bitcoin Sports Network. I participated in the _Inaugural Max & Stacy Bitcoin Golf Invitational at El Encanto, El Salvador January 2025_. Not only did I teach instruction at the event but I played in it and won a customized Bitcoin sand wedge & head covers. Visiting ES was an incredible and at a perfect time in my life. My fiancé and I are planning to create a hostel/wellness compound in the future, the black sands of El Zonte may be the location. Plan your work, Work your Plan! We will be back in ES for the 2nd Max & Stacy Golf Invite in January 2026. See you at The Ark!

Looking forward to connecting with the Tribe.
**_Cheers to being Human!_
Matt**

# Thread: Hello from Wisconsin / Visiting El Salvador on Wednesday Oct 29
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-from-wisconsin-visiting-el-salvador-on-wednesday-oct-29.31783/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 16
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### BenWCam — 2025-10-26T17:29:18+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/hello-from-wisconsin-visiting-el-salvador-on-wednesday-oct-29.31783/post-361636>

Hi everyone my name is Benjamin Cameron. I am a carpenter, natural builder, and a songwriter. My wife is an expert mold inspector and remediator and she should have an account on here soon(look out for Courtney Jarman if you want to talk about mold). We live in the northern USA. A few years ago we designed and built a high efficiency off grid house with round wood timber framing and an adobe clay floor. Off grid well pump that fills a cistern that gravity feeds to the house. We grow a lot of our own food: meat chickens, hens for eggs, big no-till vegie gardens, fruit trees, berries, and more. We have been very food focused until a year ago.

After hearing a podcast with Dr. Kruse, we allowed our house to get dark after sunset as an experiement and immediately noticed changes. The most obvious was that our three year old started falling alseep all by himself once the house got dark. Before that, it was an hour of struggle to get him to lie down and be calm. He now gets me when it is time to go to bed. He ASKS to go to bed. This triggered nonstop listening of Kruse podcasts and a huge shift in perception of the playing field. This has led me to notice and understand things I didn't before. (For example: my brother who never sees the sunrise and lives mostly indoors has chronic gout.)

Because of our backgrounds, we are working on house designs that fulfil the circadian and air quality needs of humans. We are also considering how we can adjust our lives this winter to avoid sitting indoors for months. Cross country skiis will be purchased, a sauna and cold plunge will be errected, ice fishing, hiking, a more seasonal diet...

We are here to gain wisdom about how to give our two kids(4yo and 1.5yo), our 60 and 70+ year old parents, and any curious friends/neighbors the best lives possible.

I am visiting El Salvador on Wednesday October 29th until Wednesday November 4th to explore and find a place to bring my family for a winter vacation and do further scouting for property. If anyone is interested in connecting or has any suggestions for me, I am interested to hear from you.

# Thread: Cancelling Membership Difficulties
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/cancelling-membership-difficulties.31854/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 1
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### Solstice — 2025-11-09T01:41:28+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/cancelling-membership-difficulties.31854/post-362373>

Hi,

I am asking this question here as I've cancelled my gold membership on 9/22/25 but was billed in October on 10/9/22.
I emailed RE cancelling membership x2, once 10/10/25, and again on 11/4/25, both with no response.
Today, 11/8/25, I emailed [support@jackkruse.com](mailto:support@jackkruse.com) and [support@jackkruse.com](mailto:support@jackkruse.com) to inquire.

I did get an email at some point about support tickets being marked as Spam and there were issues with emails getting through.

I originally signed up for the subscription under a different email, but changed my email when setting things up on the site.

When I cancelled my membership on 10/29/25 (again), I believe I entered both email addresses.
I cancelled again 11/8/25, using both email addresses.
It's possible the membership as far as billing was listed under the original email address and I entered the new one to cancel the first time. I don't know. However I get emails to the 2nd/updated email about the pow wows and blog posts.

# Thread: Moderna and the Seizure Threshold
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/moderna-and-the-seizure-threshold.31871/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 1
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### Josh3284 — 2025-11-12T06:03:19+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/moderna-and-the-seizure-threshold.31871/post-362527>

So first on post here, and the reason I am posting it here is because I started to post the story on X and realized that X is not truly free speech and the powers that be could use it against me. My name is Josh, I am a 41 yo pharmacist that lives in Knoxville, TN, I am married to my beautiful wife who is also a pharmacist and we have 2 daughters (Lana 11 (my stepdaughter) and Charlotte 4). I worked retail pharmacy from 2008-2022, that included working for the 2 biggest chains (CVS and Walgreens) and some local independent pharmacies in North Alabama. Walgreens and I parted ways in January 2022, 2 months after my daughter was born and I was set to take paternity leave and my wife and Walgreen's parted ways in June 2022, not to get into details but we did not leave on our own accord and things were settled with lawyers outside of court. I have no love loss for the company. With that being said back to the story at hand.
So I was part of Operation Warp Speed when I worked for WAG. I haphazardly signed up for it because I'd done a tone of Flu clinics throughout my career and working in a store during Covid was nightmare (stories for years) and honestly I needed a change of scenery. Walgreen's did a terrible job of preparing its people for this operation. The Pharmacists were given several large packets (50-60 pages per packet) to read and you were pretty much taught very basics about the jab and how you were going to bill everything. I will say all of the Pharmacists knew that the jab did not stop the spread because I had a little spiel I would repeat about how the jab worked and what to do if you were exposed to Covid, blah blah blah. So Walgreen's the generous company that they are decided that if there was any of the vax left after a clinic (bottle pulled out of the freezer and thawed....don't get me started on the all the temperature BS with each Vaccine, I have stories for days about that as well) that they were going to allow their employees to come in and get the Moderna jab. So I don't catch some stray comments, the State of TN was a Moderna state in the early days of Operation Warp Speed, meaning all of the patient and staff in the LTC facilities that we serviced got the Moderna shot, Pfizer shot was available later to the public and different stores were slated for different vaccines. My wife was the pharmacy manager at one of largest distribution stores for the Pfizer shot in the area serving all the rural stores surrounding the Smoky Mountains, so I got to hear about all the issues that were had with it. Anyways, employees for WAG could come in and get a dose of Moderna first come serve until the excess for the day ran out. Walgreen's being ever so gracious realized that folks would need their second Moderna jab and made where employees could come into various locations an get their 2nd shot. The scheduler told me she needed me to work it and it was any easy shift, you give shots and talk to employees. I was a floater so I knew people at various stores so it was nice to see techs or pharmacists I had worked with and catch up. A tech I had worked with before came in for her second shot and I started with the usual questions and then we got to the "How did you do after getting your first shot?" She casually answered I had a fever and chills (normal post jab) and I had 20 seizures that night. I said did you call anyone or report this. She replied "oh yeah someone from the CDC contacted me and told me that shot lowers the seizure threshold." I asked her if she had any documentation from the CDC and she said no but they are informing some neurologists and my neurologist is aware of this. I looked at her and said are you sure you want to get this second shot, and she said "yeah I am immunocompromised and the CDC said there was nothing really I needed to worry about." I documented it and gave her the shot. Fast forward a month later, I am working at a random store and she walks in during the middle of my shift. I walk over to her and say "hey I was really concerned after giving you the last Moderna shot, did you do any better after this one than your first one?" She replied, "No I had 20 seizures that night too, but its ok, Id rather have a few seizures than die from Covid." As time progressed many pharmacists I ran into shared similar stories they had with patients and we all agreed how it was insane that there was no documentation to back this up. Looking back on this now, I was naive to think the CDC was ignorant in this. I will never forget this for the rest of my life, the very first person that I gave the Moderna shot to was this little Old Black lady in a LTC facility, I remember she was the same age as my mother at the time (67-68yo). I gave her the shot at around 9 am and I remember leaving the facility around 3 pm and before I got on the elevator I look to one of the areas where the patients would sit and watch TV and saw that lady slumped over drooling and vomit on the floor. I grabbed a nurse and got her some help and when I got back to the store where we had to process everything, I had to fill out my first VAERS report. I had been a pharmacist for nearly 11 years at this point and given hundreds if not thousands of flu shots and never had to fill one out.
Covid was a weird time, with all the shit that came from it there were a few redeeming moments where I personally got to give the powers that be the middle finger and make life long friends. One of the good things about retail pharmacy is that I had access to immunizations cards and I knew the process of giving shots and how to get around the system. One of my now closest friends was being forced to get the jab for work. He refused to get it and he was not backing down. Our wives had been friends for years and so as ladies do, they made a plan and my wife told me that Will was coming in to the pharmacy and that “he needed the shot” which was code for he’s not getting the shot but make it look like it. So I did this for him twice (the first time was the first time we had ever met). Fast forward several months and my wife and I get a text from our friends wife saying she has to take him to the ER because she thinks he has a kidney. She tells us not to worry and that they were halfway joking about it at dinner because their youngest daughter started crying thinking her daddy was gonna die, we have a little laugh and go to sleep. I wake up the next message to a text and VM from his frantic wife because he has been admitted to the ICU for blood clots, she needed us to watch the youngest daughter while she went back to the hospital. I had to entertain a 6 yo and comfort her while her dad was receiving a slow drip of clot busters to save his life. He made a 100% recovery, but would had his fate been the same if I would have been those needles in his arm and not the trash. The doctors told him they did not know what caused the clot, but he knew and we all knew, he tested positive for Covid several weeks prior. To add insult to injury he had to be on Xarelto for several months after the fact and his PBM would not approve a PA for the meds because who knows why. Luckily his wife is a NP and had access to samples at her office. I know that he and his family are thankful, I am thankful that he was not taken out by the DOD weapon. So many more thousand…millions…of innocent people and families did not have that same outcome. So I have to tell this next quick story because ironically the guy texted me while I was writing this. My chiropractor had a fellow chiropractor friend that lived in Canada and he was trying to escape to the US to escape the tyranny of his government. At this point Canada was so locked down that they were requiring vax cards to leave the country. I told my new friend where I was working that day and what time to come see me. I remember it was early in the morning because the sun had not fully come up, and my friend showing up to the pharmacy with his wife and 4 kids. He was so nervous, a cop was grabbing a snack in the store and he looked at me and said do you think he knows. I chuckled and told him everything would be ok, the police officers in our area were probably just as opposed to the jab as he was. I shuffled the 6 of them in that small vaccine room and I didn’t even draw up any shots, I handed him the vaccine cards and told them not to worry about anything. Now here is the part of the story that not many people know. So for every Covid vaccine the pharmacies had paperwork that had to be filled out and then that paperwork had to be scanned in under the patients profile so it could be loaded up to the state database so they could track the shots and give you a digital vax card. Well that was just fear porn, because just at that store there were stacks of paperwork that had not been scanned in yet and the real kicker is that after two weeks the vaccine record would fall out of the que at the local store, so the insurance company knew you had been vaccinated but not the state database. Too add insult to injury, there was not an accurate record for anyone in the state of Tennessee when it comes to vaccines. People would ask me to check their records and a handful of vaccines from years prior would show up but hardly any recent vaccines. I looked up my own records and I believe it had some childhood vaccines my mom got at the health dept when I was a baby, but nothing else. So when you went to get on a flight and you were nervous because they were checking some database, it was all to make you scared. Plus to get access to those databases you have to have either a state license or an NPI depending on the state. I did this for several other people, I honestly wish I could have done this for more people however I am glad that time in my life is over. I am glad to have found Dr. Jack and his work. For me the mitochondriach path will not be an easy one because I am having to untangle the web of lies I was taught in Pharmacy school, but a great artist said
“If there were no rewards to reap
No loving embrace to see me through
This tedious path I've chosen here
I certainly would've walked away
By now.”
I appreciate your work Dr. Jack and if you do read this I do have 2 questions. 1) In regards to the jab and lowering the seizure threshold is this an ADR of the jab that you were aware of? And I wasn’t going to ask this but my curiosity is kicking in, do you know the mechanism/pathway that causes this and I apologize if you have already explained this, I know you are not a librarian and I can look this up on my own time. 2) I know that you did work with patents in regards to the Pfizer jab, did you look at the Moderna ones as well and is there a reason that you never hear about the Moderna jab in the press.
Thank you again

Hello everybody!
My woman Ro and me, Urko, came to the Gambia July 26th 2025 after a several discussion in November 2023 when we read the Invisible Rainbow book and started following dr Jack Kruse. We were living in 43rd latitude in the north of Spain inside the deeper basque country. We enjoyed a really nice journey in a place full of nature and cold but really lack of sun, too much clouds and a lot of issues with the local police officer that were a pain in the ass for all the people living there.

Some of the arguments that took us here were:
\- UV the whole year
\- Balanced light and dark cycles (here around 12-12h)
\- Less technologically developed place in terms of artificial light and EMF (still there are many antennas here but we deal with less populated areas than EU)
\- Do need to wear much clothes
\- Can be barefooted 100% of the time
\- Close to the sea
\- Good fish + food
\- Run away from the surveillance EU regulations and digital ID thing
\- Still in similar TZ as EU to work with my regular customers and do not loose the remote jobs I have

I'm really pleased to be on this forum I've just purchased the gold membership and I hope I can start using it but don't have enough time yet as we are on the way looking to purchase a land where we set up, we are still living in a tent I have posted many videos of our journey in our [private selfhosted peertube instance](https://tv.atalayacomunidad.org/w/p/hwUNZpnNezSb5Fqe742EFN)

Hello everyone,

My name is Tim. I’m currently in Patagonia, Argentina, but I’m actively orienting toward warmer latitudes closer to the equator.

I’m not new to Jack’s work, and I’m not here to debate theory. I’m here because I’m interested in building real-world systems that align with the biology we talk about here.

My background and interests are practical:
\- soil regeneration and mineral cycling
\- biochar (small-scale, appropriate tech, low-input systems)
\- food production infrastructure
\- working with land-based projects rather than extracting from them

I’m looking for people who are actually doing something on the ground — farms, land projects, experimental builds, or communities where biology, light, water, and food are taken seriously.

I’m location-flexible, but climate matters. I function best in warm, high-light environments and am currently exploring options in Central America and southern Mexico.

If anyone here is involved in land-based projects, regenerative food systems, or experimental builds near the equator — or knows people who are — I’d be glad to connect.

Not looking for ideology. Looking for alignment and work.

# Thread: Land, Jurisdiction, and Exit-from-Speculation — TDF & OASA (Portugal)
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/land-jurisdiction-and-exit-from-speculation-%E2%80%94-tdf-oasa-portugal.32041/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 1
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### Balfi — 2025-12-24T05:02:35+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/land-jurisdiction-and-exit-from-speculation-%E2%80%94-tdf-oasa-portugal.32041/post-364185>

Hey Mitos!

I wanted to surface a land-based experiment that may be of interest to people here who think about decentralization beyond screens and protocols.

It’s called Traditional Dream Factory (TDF), based in Alentejo, Portugal, and it sits within a broader framework called OASA. The project is still in the build-out phase, but they’ve already made meaningful strides: securing land, putting legal and governance structures in place, starting regeneration work, and actively hosting people on site.

At a high level, TDF is a physical location — an old poultry farm property plus surrounding land — being converted into a regenerative coliving and stewardship village. OASA is the higher-order structure based in Switzerland designed to make sure land doesn’t quietly drift back into speculation or extraction over time, even if founders leave or conditions change.

Access is time-based rather than equity-based, with participants holding use-rights instead of ownership or shares. Instead of ownership or shares, participants hold use-rights. Governance emphasizes presence, contribution, and stewardship rather than absentee ownership or purely financial weight. The stated long-term goal is an exit to the commons, not an exit to liquidity.

One concrete detail that helps ground this: two TDF tokens correspond to one night’s stay in one of their future apartments. That right renews every year indefinitely and isn’t “used up.” The stay can be redeemed by the holder or gifted to a friend, rather than being structured around speculation or resale pressure.

I’m personally invested in the project. I’m sharing this not as a pitch, but because I’m genuinely interested in whether this kind of model can work over time. In a bigger picture sense, I’d like to see something like this succeed well enough that it can be adapted elsewhere — potentially even for a future land-based project of my own in the US. I’m currently scouting hot spring land in Oregon, so I’m paying close attention to how these governance and stewardship questions play out in reality.

One aspect I find especially interesting is jurisdiction. TDF and OASA are more thought-through here than most decentralized land efforts I’ve seen, but the real question is still where legitimate judgment lives when norms are violated, and how consequence is enforced without collapsing into either chaos or bureaucracy. That’s something only time and stress can really validate.

Posting this mainly as a pointer for people thinking about sovereignty at the land layer, not just the monetary one. Curious how others here think about land, decentralization, and jurisdiction beyond screens.

For reference:
traditionaldreamfactory.com
oasa.earth
Sam Delesque (podcasts / talks)


══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

# Thread: Excited to learn more from all the savages out there - looking for advice
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/excited-to-learn-more-from-all-the-savages-out-there-looking-for-advice.32165/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 9
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### LiamS — 2026-01-21T09:48:00+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/excited-to-learn-more-from-all-the-savages-out-there-looking-for-advice.32165/post-365678>

I'm a University of Toronto student in my second year, though I'm barely attending lectures at this point. This forum, verified individuals and the resources online are fantastic (if people my age up here could be more discerning)! I love researching and was enthralled to find Dr. Kruse's work after doing a paper on circadian rythm in high school.

I feel stuck. I'm getting as much sun as possible sun and managing my sleep, and eating paleolitically to the best of my ability. Trying hard to manage EMF exposure with little control of my living situation due to finances.

Not a single person, with the exception of my father, knows anything about Dr. Kruse or related research. It is very isolating but I keep in mind the point about focusing on the 13%; the savages. And I'd really appreciate some help.

I fell in with the wrong crowd. I'm addicted to vaping and smoking weed, pretty much all day. I feel terrible all the time. I initially was going to study to become a doctor, and was directed into kinesiology by peers and my guidance counselor. Now I realize it's next to impossible, and I also don't want to be a slave to the Canadian medical apparatus. My parents also have had me in front of a screen for a greater portion of my childhood. Only in the past 2 years did I start to try and change, and I've been mosyly unsuccessful. My mental health is horrible and I have really thick brain fog.

I feel paralyzed. I've got a little btc in cold storage and under 5k cad in accessible funds. I've tried endeavors in e-commerce, trading, and AI but am too poor in health and addicted to keep up. I'm basically scheduled to go work as an XR technician next summer. I want to escape this country before then, and regain my health and find some direction.

I ask of anyone for some advice and would love to connect. I'm not qualified or very talented but am trying my absolute best to become better every day. (And new to using forums, so apologies if the formality is off - I'm slowly getting through it all!)

Holler if you're in Toronto or the GTA - let's grab a coffee!

### flavin0 — 2026-01-22T05:52:28+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/excited-to-learn-more-from-all-the-savages-out-there-looking-for-advice.32165/post-365722>

I remember visiting relatives in downtown Toronto, around Queen and Spadina. It was the winter. Much colder than California. At the time I was really focusing in on keto back in 2018, 2019, eating salmon and nuts, etc. I wasn't cold walking around in a pretty minimal outfit. My relatives were kind of surprised I wasn't cold. It wasn't until this year I think I found out why.

Maybe you could find some seafood that fits your budget (maybe at the Asian markets if they have that over there) and embrace the cold.

Cheers

Welcome Liam to Uncle Jack’s tribe of savages. When I first came across him and heard him use the words tribe and savages I was in the midst of incessantly researching for answers to help my 3 year old son with a speech delay and possible adhd/autism diagnosis in addition to my daughter’s and my own health issues. When I realized that everything available to overcome these issues were bandaids and not getting to the root of the issues let alone coming up with real solutions. The basic solution is learn to live with it or take pills. I said to myself one day, screw it, I’m going to find a way to cure him (and us) myself and when I find the solutions I’ll know it because it will make perfect sense. It became my new hobby, a delightful obsession, because I know what humans are capable of with sheer will and drive. When Dr Kruse said his tribe and called them savages that’s exactly how I felt. Like a savage foaming at the mouth for answers. I even looked up the word because meaning is important. Wild, merciless, unforgiving, fierce, extreme in strength or degree. That last one, extreme in strength or degree. To what degree are you willing to go for your health, your families health, for the truth. Extreme is the right answer. That’s the kind of people Uncle Jack wants around him. You don’t have to be a brain surgeon or a rocket scientist. You don’t have to have a title. You don’t have to be wealthy. You don’t even have to be the smartest guy in the room because even that guy didn’t know squat at one point in his life. What I’m getting at is that you have to have the drive and determination to find the answers you’re looking for and more importantly, using those answers to make the right decisions for yourself. Otherwise you’re wasting his time and yours. Now I can already tell you’re smart and your Dad too for knowing who Dr. Kruse is. Don’t worry if nobody you know has ever heard of him. In my experience even when you tell them, many aren’t willing to receive it. You’re in school but it sounds like listening to other people’s advice has put you on a career path that’s not exactly what your looking for. You’re pretty health conscious but are smoking weed all day. You have a little savings but you think it’s not enough to make moves. I believe you are at a crossroads my friend. You know that you don’t like the current state of things. You especially don’t like the state of your health. And you’re honest about it. Which means there’s hope for you. Now for the advice. Honestly I don’t even like calling it advice because as soon as someone says, my advice would be…”, or “If you want my advice…”, they usually have no place giving advice on that particular subject but proceed to anyway. Or worse their delivery is horrible and the person doesn’t get the message. See most people will start telling you all the things you already know but haven’t started doing. Maybe they’ll say change your major do what you want to do, or the first thing is you gotta stop smoking weed, stop hanging out with that crowd, or maybe even give you a job or venture idea but if you’re not thinking like a savage you won’t follow through. Dr Kruse mentioned he had a mentor that was tough and if he had an issue his mentor would say “so what” as if to say figure it out. Here we all get Dr Kruse as a mentor and he’s tough. He’s not going to hold your hand one, because he would be doing you a disservice, but two, because you have to take control of your destiny. His immense library of information is there for the taking. But you have to take the time to get his gift of time: your health. With your health the sky’s the limit. And just because you put in the time doesn’t mean it will be easy and the clock will still be ticking. I can give you suggestions but you have to want the change and be fiercely determined to make it happen, even through the brain fog. The more you read, listen, and learn you can implement changes that will incrementally make your circumstances better. It’s hard to know where to start but I listen to a lot of his interviews, many of them multiple times and some notes. The forum, of course, and his blogs and papers. I too have mental blocks such as focus issues, brain fog, retention problems but I don’t let that stop me. If I have to read something multiple times so be it. His earlier stuff I’m learning now is a good place to start. You could write down what changes you want to make in your life, then put them in order of significance, than write out what you need to do to get there. That makes it more real and achievable. For example if you want to stop smoking because maybe it’s causing or worsening your brain fog which then makes decision making hard, write out what you can do to implement that such as walking or running when you want to smoke or go to the library to read where you can’t smoke. Most importantly love yourself and know that your health and happiness is worth putting in the time. Things will start to fall in place and opportunities will arise in the most unexpected places. I’m rooting for you Liam!

### Anthony Smith — 2026-01-23T06:46:51+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/excited-to-learn-more-from-all-the-savages-out-there-looking-for-advice.32165/post-365771>

Temperature has nothing to do with grounding - just comfort.
A good ground has NO nnEMF 60Hz (50Hz) electric field running through it.
So, the further away from buildings, industry, technology etc. you are the better off you will be.
The equipment to test the ground for these 50/60hz fields is not readily available.
A body voltage meter will show IF the surface you are standing on is grounded BUT not if that ground is “clean”.
In town, at your home look for utility lines . . . Avoid them.
IF you are in a city, good chance the ground is not “clean”.
Grounding in Nature is amazing/great . . . If you want to ground in Nature . . . Be in Nature.

# Thread: Guy's Journal
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/guys-journal.32382/>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 1
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### Guy Houri — 2026-03-13T12:31:38+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/guys-journal.32382/post-368694>

Hi all! Been on the forum for a while - thought I should post a few words about myself, and keep updating on my journey

### **ZIPCODE** - Tel Aviv, Israel, 33N​

**Political Status**
I know Israel is a controversial place lol, my view about politics has completely changed after hearing Dr. Kruse. It is not so dangerous to live here IMO. My conditions are quite well overall and I am not planning on moving soon. Conditions are elaborated below:

**Finance**
I have a B.Sc. in Computer Science and am currently Fiat Farming as a Data Engineer. Work from home 3 days a week (2 days at office). Home is at a wired desk, full sun & naked, pretty awesome. Stacking BTC. Maybe should put it for yield and make more money, or find more side hustles I have in mind, when I'll get more time.

**Sun, Cold, EMF, Food**

-   **Sun** - I have a great tan here; it didn't fade in the winter months. Though next winter I definitely should take a vacation because I felt the lack of sun in my mood. Have red lights in my room at night, blue blockers, and tons of 100W incandescents.
-   **Cold** - Honestly, only in December-January there is not a lot of sunshine but other than that I'm shirtless outside every day. I think I am not cold adapted; I have done many ice baths during the winter at a local gym (cancelled the membership now and planning on setting up one at home). I always feel nice in the bath but I overdid it a few times and felt bad afterwards. Should have done more walks outside shirtless but it was difficult mentally, and it takes time - so I need to work on that.
-   **EMFs** - I live in the suburbs and very low EMFs. My room is in the basement and I have none. I bought Dirty Electricity filters. Have a Cornet, Multimeter, and an ESMOG meter. Direct phone calls to computer (Phone on airplane mode), wired headphones, etc.
-   **Food** - Mostly Keto. Buying mussels/sardines from iHerb / cheap Russian supermarkets nearby. Meal 1: half avocado, 2 Omega-3 eggs, 2 packs of sardines, olive oil, lemon, radish, turnip. Second meal might be fish. Third meal maybe mussels, radish, and an egg. Sometimes I break the diet and as an excuse I continue to eat all the things I avoided and binge a bit. Need to work on that. Some foods also don't sit well with me, so sometimes I have to change up the meal plan.

### **History / About Me**​

23 yrs old. Always went kind of against the grain, and was not afraid to be different. Liked to hike as a kid but wore sunscreen and been on screens. A few years ago I got into optimizing my health. Heard a bunch of Huberman stuff. Overall if I am being honest I do not really feel improvements since implementing the protocols. Being a black swan has its social disadvantages as well. But I am happy that I saw the light. Perhaps the luckiest day of my life was accidentally clicking on the J. Kruse-Huberman podcast. Life-changing. I do feel happier in summer I think. But then again I am not always 100% on the protocols as well, but overall I am not sick.

**Medical History**
No major health issues, overall feeling good. Winter kind of sucked if I'm being honest but my living conditions improved drastically since (sun and EMF), I am very lucky to have what I have. I did get all the vaccines unfortunately, and as a kid had screen time etc.. I am half Iraqi from my father's side, and my mother's side is from Europe. Tbh Jewish heritage is a bit harder to track but I have blue eyes and my base is white skin though it won't be recognized haha. I have some small stuff that is still bothering me, but that's life I guess.

**Social**
I am extroverted, but I don't find it interesting to have conversations with normies so much haha.
Haven't quite found my people yet. Have only one friend who I Kruse-Pilled. The others are still half-believers with dopamine issues.
Last year visited ES and had a great time. But job/family-social situation in Israel is better for me.

### **Future Goals and Thoughts**​

I am still building my spiritual belief system, don't know where I am on the spectrum. (Is God real? Do we have souls? Questions that are on my mind).
Haven't found purpose focusing only on optimizing my health. Feeling a bit too self centered. Still don't know how I should be spreading more light to the world.
Wondering if and how I will be able to build a decentralized community and family.
All I know is I'll be following nature, and try my best.

Grateful to be a part of this community.

# Thread: How to watch the sunrise and sunset?
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/how-to-watch-the-sunrise-and-sunset.32606/unread>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 10
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### Millerstef — 2026-04-22T01:27:16+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/how-to-watch-the-sunrise-and-sunset.32606/post-371758>

Hello. I am brand new here and I have been searching the site for this question because it seemed so basic and surely it would have been discussed. I live in Portland Oregon, 1 hour plus from the ocean, however I am very close to the Willamette River. I am on the East side of it so if I was on the shore facing the river I would be facing west. Is this a fine place to watch the sunrise and sunset? Also, if sunrise is at 6:15 a.m. what time I should I plan to get there. Dawn starts at 5:45. If I can't get down to the river can I just go out to my lawn with my feet in the grass? From my house I don't have a great view of the sky due to all the trees. I would love some guidance in this department if someone doesn't mind sharing how they do sunrise and sunset if they do not have access to the ocean. Thank you.

### MTA321 — 2026-04-22T02:08:45+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/how-to-watch-the-sunrise-and-sunset.32606/post-371765>

I wouldn’t over think it that much. Just get outside, have bare feet on the ground and look in the direction of the sun. Even if you have obstructions, the ambient light should be just fine.

### Millerstef — 2026-04-22T02:26:03+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/how-to-watch-the-sunrise-and-sunset.32606/post-371768>

> [MTA321 said:](/goto/post?id=371765)
>
> I wouldn’t over think it that much. Just get outside, have bare feet on the ground and look in the direction of the sun. Even if you have obstructions, the ambient light should be just fine.

I appreciate your response. Do you go outside while it is still dark? Just trying to set up my morning to make it happen since sunrise is quite early here. I was hoping for clarity, if sunrise is 6:45 tomorrow is that what time I head out or prior when it is still dusk. Thanks

### MattB99 — 2026-04-22T05:02:17+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/how-to-watch-the-sunrise-and-sunset.32606/post-371793>

After watching sunrises for a while I tend to wake up automatically at daybreak. No need to set an alarm. Assuming your bedroom gets natural light.

### digitald3 — 2026-04-22T05:36:15+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/how-to-watch-the-sunrise-and-sunset.32606/post-371794>

Don’t over think it. Just get outside with bare feet on the ground sometime before the sunrises and if possible stay out until the UVA rise which is usually about an hour after sunrise. But if you can’t don’t sweat it and maybe take a break at that time and go for a sun break. Mountain, trees, clouds don’t matter

### Mr.AJ — 2026-04-22T16:38:35+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/how-to-watch-the-sunrise-and-sunset.32606/post-371835>

I get outside sometime after it is light out but before the sun is visible to me. Not sure if this is exactly optimal but it's working for me.

### Anthony Smith — 2026-04-22T19:27:47+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/how-to-watch-the-sunrise-and-sunset.32606/post-371847>

The problem for most of going out while it is still dark is the artificial light you become exposed to, both in the home and from street light etc.

My personal choice is to be out a few mins before sun rise and stay as long as that days events allow. Avoid ALL artificial light.

### Evee — 2026-05-01T00:37:14+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/heliotrope-rash.32671/post-372685>

So I'm awaiting testing, but I have what looks to be a heliotrope rash, which is pretty indicative of dermatomyositis.

So clearly, I need to leave where I am, and taking long trips to Mexico and El Salvador has not been enough to offset living in the US.

Unfortunately, in the most immediate future, I'm going to have to do a lot of testing to rule out paraneoplastic syndrome which is associated with dermatomyositis.

But something is driving me crazy about how this disease is counseled. They tell people to stay out of the sun to avoid setting off an immune cascade. For the record, I will NOT stay out of the sun.
But I'm trying to understand, if inflammation is there because there's an antibody attacking something, it's not attacking ghosts, right? There must be some trigger?

So I understand in paraneoplastic syndrome, it's a response to the tumor, but for non-cancer dermatomyositis there still must be some trigger(s), no?

Some of markers they talk about are the same as mold (mmp9) so if Shoemaker can reverse an inflammatory cascade with a protocol or you can heal mold by renovating your melanin in a good environment, WHY wouldn't there be some way to reverse a cascade with this? Or am I thinking too simply?

I'm including a screenshot of the rationale they give for staying out of the sun. I don't know enough about how the immune system works to argue with that, I just know, following Uncle Jack's advice is the ONLY thing that has ever helped me. I felt the best I ever felt in Quintana Roo where I HEALED Hell's Itch on my shoulder (only other thing I did was a visit to an osteopath so maybe that helped too) but Hell's Itch is another thing they tell you not go in the sun with, but I got BETTER in the sun.

I'm sorry if these questions are dense, I was working like 7 days a week before all this started and I'm horribly behind on blogs, mostly following on the forum and podcasts. If there a blog series I should start back in with I will or I'll just pick a place and start.

### WvMts — 2026-05-03T19:41:32+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/newish-silver-member.32689/post-372923>

Been lurking awhile. Figured I better post something about myself and say hi. So much to learn. Raised outside of Philly ( don't hold it against me, lol) currently in WV. I've done ultrasound since1995 but moved in 2000 to rural WV because I hated the city and always wanted to homestead. When you scan someone you are alone with them in the dark ( with only a blue light screen smh..) but its like a confessional and people tell you all sorts of things . At the time I was a cardiac tech so the scans took awhile.. #1 was the regret they didn't do what they really wanted to do and put off things for retirement. But then found they were too sick to do any of them. So I took their advice and moved to try and do what I was more passionate about. So I've been here for 26 yrs and never regretted moving. We raise our own grassfed beef and chicken and can garden. We have a well . I still work in ultrasound but I've cut my hours back dramatically because I know that environment is literally killing me but it pays the bills. Now learning about the magnetic declination I feel like it's year 2000 again, but I'm older and not so brave. I renewed my passport and I want to visit El Salvador to at least see for myself what it's like and if I think my pale gringo ass could make it work. Having a bunch of livestock and critters does make even taking a vacation complicated but I'm determined to figure something out. I am thankful to have this forum to learn from. Hopefully I can contribute more eventually, but right now I am still riding the short bus on most things so I'm reading as much as I can.

# Thread: *help needed to navigate this space* New Gold member - adrenal fatigue, thyroiditis/hypothyroid, chronic fatigue (ex vegan, now carnivore)
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/help-needed-to-navigate-this-space-new-gold-member-adrenal-fatigue-thyroiditis-hypothyroid-chronic-fatigue-ex-vegan-now-carnivore.32730/unread>
**Subforum:** Meet and Greet
**Posts:** 1
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### Beccy — 2026-05-09T23:34:29+0300
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/help-needed-to-navigate-this-space-new-gold-member-adrenal-fatigue-thyroiditis-hypothyroid-chronic-fatigue-ex-vegan-now-carnivore.32730/post-373580>

Hi, I am almost 50, was vegan for 12 years, had a lifetime of allergies, IBS, chronic fatigue, pernicious anaemia, and a passion and drive for a profession which is extremely physically and mentally challenging (travelling equine podiatrist consultant and coach). I have tried dozens of diet and healing protocols and never felt I have achieved anything close to my potential to be well, and therefore have never felt I had the resources to fulfill my life’s purpose. The will to do so keeps me seeking answers and solutions and fighting the good fight for optimum health and wellness for optimum longevity.

I am currently 135lb, eat mostly lamb, salt and spring water, and am 5 foot 4 inches. I am self employed and have slowed down my schedule this year due to my stressful career since December in order to prioritise healing. I dont drink alcohol or smoke.

Since radically changing my diet, most of previous chronic and periodically acute symptoms have gone, such as IBS.

My biggest challenges currently are energy, consistent sleep, or a lack of both, brain fog and memory issues. I wish to be creative and productive, fit and active once more, and yes, wear my clothes comfortably without the extra pounds gained in the past few years. I wish to contribute more to supporting my family….

What got me here…

I had my last gallbladder attack 10th Dec 2025, and then started IF (16:8) and slowly switched to paleo with meat over the next 6 weeks. I experienced the keto high in January, lost 10lbs and felt great. Then crashed. On 1st March, I went pure carnivore, stopped drinking caffeine and taking progesterone HRT. I had 4 weeks of sleep hell and zombie energy, and from 1st April, received support from a carnivore naturopath who recommended 4 part saliva cortisol and more thyroid tests (I had them done in February and realised I was hypo and inflamed - “on the away to Hashimotos“. I discovered I am low cortisol - but following correct daily curve, just low. The naturopath recommended natural desiccated thyroid and adrenal cortex supplements and these Increased energy and function literally overnight. This was In April. My thyroid T3 level is normal anccording to repeat blood test early May and I haven’t re-tested saliva yet.

I found this site after exploring why I am gaining weight again (not muscle - fat/water) and have worrying lymphedemia - this is eased by rebounding and daily lymphatic massage on 7 key points. I lost 8lbs in 24 hours by doing this. However I am not getting any additional info from the carnivore community I am in and am very dedicated to regaining my health and life, and achieve my life goals. I also know I feel better in the sun, hence my attraction to the work Dr Kruse does and melanin.

I live in northern England. I try and sunbathe (naked) whenever I can, and I practice good sleep hygiene. I recently tracking health stuff with a Hume pod and wearable device for better objectivity in my health.

I am keen to learn and somewhat overwhelmed by all this new and complicated information.

\* How do I use the membership best to begin to navigate my way to health? I am overwhelmed \*

That’s me!
